data-rawheight=\"350\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"781\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-09ab8a488f9feea39eb75ca84ac4048b_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-09ab8a488f9feea39eb75ca84ac4048b_b.jpg\"/></figure></b><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>从拾雨交易记录可大体算出本周拾雨的盈利情况：若都是做一手，则16.5×7×100=11550美元利润，其中还去掉了拾雨亏损的一单1×（-3）×100=300美元；若是10手呢，则是16.5×7×10×100=115500美元利润，当然这还要扣除手续费。因此只要跟上拾雨做单，盈利不再是梦，这还是本周行情不大，一直在1220-1232期间震荡的结果。　　</b></p><p><b>在来看一下下周展望：　　</b></p><p><b>据中国海关总署最新发布的数据显示，今年前3季度，我国以人民币计价的进出口总额达22.28万亿元，同比增长9.9%，此外，中国和美国贸易也仍然活跃。前3季度，中国美国出口增长6.5%，中国对美的贸易顺差也进一步扩大，9月份中国对美国贸易顺差为341.3亿美元，创下中美贸易顺差纪录！　　</b></p><p><b>美国内部对加息也存在分歧，美国总统特/朗/普就经常批评美联储加息太急，再加上美联储内部对加息也分歧严重，旧金山联储主席布拉德(James Bullard)表示，美联储当前的货币政策可能会增加美国经济陷入衰退的风险。美国意外强劲的经济增速可能开始逐渐放缓。　　</b></p><p><b>再加上美国股市近期表现平平，美债收益率持续走低，财政赤字不断增加，财政入不敷出。让投资者对美国当前的经济堪忧，造成避险资本外逃入金市避险。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><b><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b487a8490215f88881bcf302d71c9efe_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"949\" data-rawheight=\"519\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"949\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b487a8490215f88881bcf302d71c9efe_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;949&#39; height=&#39;519&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"949\" data-rawheight=\"519\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"949\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b487a8490215f88881bcf302d71c9efe_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b487a8490215f88881bcf302d71c9efe_b.jpg\"/></figure></b><p><b>综合上述分析，那拾雨认为下周黄金有望突破1215-1235区间，实现走高期望，多头再次压制空头，本周美指连续测试96关口未能实现有效突破，也就是说投资者对美国经济增长忧虑进一步反应到美元上，那么相对美元兑黄金的压制减弱，空头后继乏力，多头有生力量还在蓄势增加。因此拾雨认为下周黄金下方支撑于1215一线左右，上方就现阶段而言1235一线阻力还是比较强势，若下周多头有生力量增加足够则会一举突破到达1245一线。　　</b></p><p><b>本周原油总结及下周展望：　　</b></p><p><b>原油方面从周一、周二震荡，周三、周四一路下挫未有回调，周五回调上行。从周初的72.26一路下滑至周四68.46美元/桶，周五微弱上涨收于69.51美元/桶。本周原油行情波动较大，按照上周一路中线空思路盈利也是相当可观的，来看一下拾雨本周原油交易日记：</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><b></b><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>从拾雨交易日记也可大体算出拾雨原油的盈亏情况：还是按一手计算9.1×1000×1=9100美元，若是10手呢，那不就是91000美元么，当然，实际盈利需要扣除手续费的。　　</b></p><p><b>国际油价周五(10月19日)盘中适度反弹约1%，美国原油库存报告的利空影响暂时消退，美元涨势受阻暂时为油价带来支撑，投资者密切关注即将公布的美国钻井数报告。美国WTI原油期货价格盘中最高触及69.76美元/桶，布伦特原油期货价格盘中最高触及80.88美元/桶。最新数据显示，上周美国原油库存大增约650万桶/日，连续第四周录得增长且远超市场预期，这令油价本周承压。　　</b></p><p><b>不过沙特失踪记者事件依然引发投资者对中东局势的担心，结合临近第二轮伊朗制裁的实施日期，原油供应面恐面临更大的挑战，这为油价提供有效支撑。美国总统已经表态，如果确认记者卡舒吉事件与沙特王室有关，必然实施强力惩罚。另一方面，美国计划在11月4日实施第二轮伊朗制裁，但有人指出，沙特和俄罗斯的原油增产有可能会填补伊朗供应空缺，这令油市的不确定性攀升。　　</b></p><p><b>拾雨认为，市场供应水平保持不变，而现在又处于一年当中炼厂进行维护的时期，我们还需将注意力转向美国11月初重新实施对伊朗的制裁后，该国的原油出口将会大幅下降；沙特本月表示，将每天增产30万桶，以帮助抵消伊朗下月原油出口骤降造成的供应缺口；但是我仍对任何一个国家是否有足够的闲置产能来弥补伊朗原油供应的缺失持怀疑态度。　</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><b><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d983c5ed5cb393c9ac633772ac8fbea9_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1034\" data-rawheight=\"602\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1034\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d983c5ed5cb393c9ac633772ac8fbea9_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1034&#39; height=&#39;602&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1034\" data-rawheight=\"602\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1034\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d983c5ed5cb393c9ac633772ac8fbea9_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d983c5ed5cb393c9ac633772ac8fbea9_b.jpg\"/></figure></b><p><b>综合上述分析，拾雨个人对于下周原油整体上是看涨，首先说道美国EIA库存应该已经足够，为了清空其原油库存，美国商人不得不卖出原油，作为一个商人肯定希望价格越高越好，再次，有消息面得出，美国又在搞事了，制裁伊朗执行日期将近，再加上记者事件又有了新的目标沙特躺枪。恰好都是产油过，在我要卖油的时候搞搞你，吓唬吓唬，即耍了威风又让我的东西可以高价卖出何乐而不为呢。因此拾雨对于下周原油激进看法或会重上75，保守点看法72.5-73一线遇阻力回撤。　　</b></p><p><b>下周重要财经数据及财经大事需要重点关注：　　</b></p><p><b>1.2018年票委、亚特兰大联储主席博斯蒂克发表讲话;2.美国10月里奇蒙德联储制造业指数;3.美国至10月19日当周API原油库存;4.欧元区10月制造业PMI初值;5美国8月FHFA房价指数月率;6美国10月Markit制造业PMI初值;7美国10月Markit服务业PMI初值;8.加拿大至10月24日央行利率决定公布和货币政策报告;9.美国9月新屋销售总数年化(万户);10美国至10月19日当周EIA原油库存.11.2018年FOMC票委、亚特兰大联储主席博斯蒂克就经济前景和货币政策发表讲话;12.欧元区至10月25日欧洲央行主要再融资利率；13.美国至10月20日当周初请失业金人数；14.美国9月耐用品订单月率；15.美国9月成屋签约销售指数月率；16.美国至10月19日当周EIA天然气库存；17美联储发布经济状况褐皮书；18.欧洲央行公布利率决议；19.美国第三季度实际GDP年化季率初值；20.美国第三季度实际个人消费支出季率初值；21.美国第三季度核心PCE物价指数年率初值；22.美国10月密歇根大学消费者信心指数终值；23.美联储副主席克拉里达(Richard Clarida)就经济前景发表讲话；24欧洲央行行长德拉基(Mario Draghi)在“了解通胀动能：成本的角色、涨价和预期”会议结束时发表主题演说。　　</b></p><p><b>文章由李拾雨撰写，以上内容仅供参考，仅代表个人观点，文章时效性较强，具有滞后性，具体操作以实盘为准，投资有风险，入市需谨慎。　　</b></p><p><b>谢谢阅读！</b></p>",

            "title": "第284期：poke the bear", 
            "content": "<p>今天我们来学一个跟熊有关的词，都很有趣，很形象，也很容易记住: Poke the bear.</p><p>Poke the bear, 通常用作否定形式：Don&#39;t poke the bear. 意思是“别没事儿找事儿”，No zuo no die; don&#39;t ask for trouble; Don&#39;t look for trouble.</p><p>英语释义：To  poke the bear is to do something that might provoke someone into  becoming angry or causing problems.  也有人把这个俗语直译为“戳熊”的，佛老觉得如果非要直译的话，不如译为“惹熊”更好。</p><p>Poke的意思是“戳”，想象一个场景：一头熊正在睡觉，你从它身边走过，本来没事。你偏要捡一根树枝去戳它。它醒来会怎样？（此处略去283字）</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-52eea7bda41fef430a9a1cb8d91c2f83_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"705\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-52eea7bda41fef430a9a1cb8d91c2f83_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;705&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"705\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-52eea7bda41fef430a9a1cb8d91c2f83_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-52eea7bda41fef430a9a1cb8d91c2f83_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>Bears are lovely creatures that often hibernate and are, for the most part, non-violent. However, when poked, bears can become quite angry. As such, it&#39;s always best <b>not</b> to poke the bear.</p><p>来看Urban Dictionary上的一个例句：</p><p>Employee 1: &#34;Should I ask the boss for a day off?&#34; 员工1：我应该找老板请一天假吗？<br/> Employee 2: &#34;He just found out his wife left him, so don&#39;t poke the bear.&#34; 员工2： 他老婆刚离开他，还是别去惹熊了。</p><p>怎么样，是不是很形象？</p><p>Graham Allison教授的新书&#34;Destined for war&#34;中有这样一段对中苏1969年边界珍宝岛战争的描述，用了poke the bear，很棒。大家来欣赏一下。</p><p>Still, facing an angry Soviet Union, Mao adopted an unexpected strategy: <b><u>he poked the bear</u></b>.</p><p>China&#39;s  military planned an attack that would &#34;strive for suddenness of action&#34;  and teach Moscow a &#34;bitter lesson.&#34; On March 2, 1969, the PLA ambushed  Soviet border troops on Zhenbao island in the Ussuri River, followed  shortly by a second attack, killing ninety-one Soviets at the cost of  thirty Chinese.</p><p>佛老觉得上面这段对M的描写用了he poked the bear不仅成语用的恰当，而且用bear来指代苏俄，一语双关，词趣盎然。绝妙的一句话。</p><p>*原文发布于：</p><a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//giraffenglish.net/2018/10/19/poke-the-bear/\" data-draft-node=\"block\" data-draft-type=\"link-card\" data-image=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-741a3e8b62c011cbf7f4d22715683300_180x120.jpg\" data-image-width=\"594\" data-image-height=\"252\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">第284期：poke the bear - 長頸鹿英語</a><p></p>",

            "content": "<p>黄金分析：</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-d56552cc56fa1fdc4944ed0b59dc78fe_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"630\" data-rawheight=\"433\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"630\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-d56552cc56fa1fdc4944ed0b59dc78fe_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;630&#39; height=&#39;433&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"630\" data-rawheight=\"433\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"630\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-d56552cc56fa1fdc4944ed0b59dc78fe_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-d56552cc56fa1fdc4944ed0b59dc78fe_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>黄金目前暂缓本周的回撤，由两周半低位上升至100日SMA附近，逼近1225美元区域。美元正挣扎于构筑近两周高位附近的积极动能，这成为以美元计价的黄金持续吸引买盘兴趣的重要原因。　　</p><p>加上股票市场普遍的谨慎情绪反映出投资者风险情绪的恶化，以及对于中美贸易展的担忧为黄金的避险天堂需求提供了助力。　　</p><p>美联储一位重要官员周四表示，尽管美国经济的生产能力可能在增加，但美联储最好还是继续稳步加息，直到有确凿证据。他表示，对生产力提升持怀疑态度，越来越少的理由支撑加快加息。可能在数据显示出强烈信号之后，美联储才会调整当先“稳定、渐进且可预见的”加息节奏。有能力在没有限制性的情况下渐进式加息。　</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-e7d9ddd653451ea322a8815776e3dab3_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"981\" data-rawheight=\"376\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"981\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-e7d9ddd653451ea322a8815776e3dab3_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;981&#39; height=&#39;376&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"981\" data-rawheight=\"376\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"981\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-e7d9ddd653451ea322a8815776e3dab3_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-e7d9ddd653451ea322a8815776e3dab3_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>黄金也在测试100日移动均线切入位附近的阻力位1226美元左右，突破该水准可能引发进一步上涨，并对空头施压。　　</p><p>综合上述分析，拾雨对于今日黄金看法任然震荡偏上行，其震荡区间1220-1230.早间黄金或会先上涨至1229附近遇阻力下跌至1220附近。因此日内操作拾雨建议高空为主，低多为辅，现价1226多单进场，目标1229-1230.，观望突破情况，若回调则空单进场，目标1222-1220一线。　　</p><p>原油分析：</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-9ca6d623af091964e1443f723149f15e_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"505\" data-rawheight=\"395\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"505\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-9ca6d623af091964e1443f723149f15e_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;505&#39; height=&#39;395&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"505\" data-rawheight=\"395\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"505\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-9ca6d623af091964e1443f723149f15e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-9ca6d623af091964e1443f723149f15e_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>美国能源信息署(EIA)周三(10月17日)公布报告显示，截至10月12日当周，美国原油库存增加649万桶至4.164亿桶，连续4周录得增长，市场预估为增加216.7万桶。更多数据显示，上周俄克拉荷马州库欣原油库存增加177.6万桶，连续4周录得增长。　　</p><p>美国油服公司贝克休斯(Baker Hughes)周五(10月12日)公布数据显示，截至10月12日当周，美国石油活跃钻井数增加8座至869座，四周来首次录得增长，创8月中旬以来最大单周增幅。更多数据显示，截至10月12日当周美国石油和天然气活跃钻井总数增加11座至1063座。　　</p><p>国际能源署(IEA)在月报中指出，国际货币基金组织(IMF)下调经济增长预期是下调原油需求预期的原因。除此之外，随着委内瑞拉和伊朗等国供应量下降的情况恶化，其他产油国备用产能将仅占全球需求的2%，并可能会进一步萎缩。IEA同时指出，石油输出国组织(OPEC)、俄罗斯以及其他主要产油国自5月以来已经大幅增产，今年可能会增产140万桶/日。　　</p><p>价周四下跌，因投资者再次担心中美贸易争端升级将对石油需求增长产生影响，且数据显示供应充足；，此轮回调的真正推动力是对需求增长和贸易问题的担忧，世界已经从周期的波峰回落；美国炼油厂进入维护季，期间主要工厂停产四至六周，这也打压了原油需求和价格；供应水平保持不变，而现在又处于一年当中炼厂进行维护的时期；投资者还将注意力转向，美国11月初重新实施对伊朗的制裁后，该国的原油出口将会大幅下降；沙特本月表示，将每天增产30万桶，以帮助抵消伊朗下月原油出口骤降造成的供应缺口；投资者仍对任何一个国家是否有足够的闲置产能来弥补伊朗原油供应的缺失持怀疑态度。　　</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c08154a72ef39379939bd7ec29758044_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"798\" data-rawheight=\"561\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"798\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c08154a72ef39379939bd7ec29758044_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;798&#39; height=&#39;561&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"798\" data-rawheight=\"561\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"798\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c08154a72ef39379939bd7ec29758044_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c08154a72ef39379939bd7ec29758044_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>综合分析;拾雨个人对原油今日看法任然是看空，因上周美国原油产量大幅下降主要是受到飓风气候影响，因此不会持续，本周原油产量有望回升，这令原油多头信心受到打压。　　</p><p>4小时图显示，油价目前承压于云图下行云下方，且下行云正处于不断走低的趋势中。MA均线呈空头排列趋势，RSI触及超卖水平，这表明油价短线的下行趋势较为明显。上方70.5已经转化为较强的阻力，升破该位置前，后市偏向下行；若意外在该位置上方停留较长时间，则削弱短线看空信号。　　</p><p>从周线级别来看，油价目前正在测试20周均线支撑，跌穿这一支撑，那么油价有望下探40周均线在67.50美元附近的支撑，油价自2017年10月13日以来基本交投该均线上方，因此一旦跌穿这一均线的话，那么很可能意味着中期上涨走势将要逆转。因此，原油日内操作拾雨建议高空为主，低多为辅，早间68.7左右做多，目标69.5附近，遇阻下落做空，目标看至67-67.5一线支撑。　　</p><p>日内重要财经数据及财经大事仍需要关注，周五谨防黑天鹅！！！　</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4830cdf3bb01b190b4a1e5873b224390_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"810\" data-rawheight=\"754\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"810\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4830cdf3bb01b190b4a1e5873b224390_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;810&#39; height=&#39;754&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"810\" data-rawheight=\"754\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"810\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4830cdf3bb01b190b4a1e5873b224390_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4830cdf3bb01b190b4a1e5873b224390_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>文章由李拾雨撰写，以上内容仅供参考，仅代表个人观点，文章时效性较强，具有滞后性，具体操作以实盘为准，投资有风险，入市需谨慎。　　</p><p>谢谢阅读！</p>",

            "title": "李拾雨：欧盟峰会脱欧进展不力，英镑再度面临打压，黄金再获支撑", 
            "content": "<p>　　欧盟峰会举行，商议英国脱欧协议投票表决的时候，下午欧盟官员发表看法：如果脱欧没有取得进展，或将举行无协议脱欧峰会。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-936e536e1b5261c5113cc87068590993_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1600\" data-rawheight=\"1102\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1600\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-936e536e1b5261c5113cc87068590993_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1600&#39; height=&#39;1102&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1600\" data-rawheight=\"1102\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1600\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-936e536e1b5261c5113cc87068590993_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-936e536e1b5261c5113cc87068590993_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>　　然欧洲理事会主席图斯克：无协定脱欧的可能性比以往更高。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>　　而英国首相发言人：相信能在秋季达成脱欧协议；仍未就脱欧的法定协议达成一致。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>　　荷兰合作银行：若11月底脱欧协议框架仍未成形，市场将开始转变为预期无协议脱欧结果，届时将引发英镑的新一轮抛售。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>　　美联储主席鲍威尔：无序脱欧将损害美国的经济。担心英国硬脱欧的溢出效应。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-053c893172902e071b47b055121a157a_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2400\" data-rawheight=\"1800\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"2400\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-053c893172902e071b47b055121a157a_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;2400&#39; height=&#39;1800&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2400\" data-rawheight=\"1800\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"2400\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-053c893172902e071b47b055121a157a_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-053c893172902e071b47b055121a157a_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>　　从种种迹象来看，此次脱欧取得进展将有限，不排除英国无协议脱欧。按照英国的说法，欧盟已拖累英国，在加上地缘政治关系，英国和欧洲大陆始终隔着一条英吉利海峡。再加上英国底蕴雄厚，毕竟称霸世界300年。因此英国加入欧盟后在欧洲获得的利益赶不上付出，欧盟提出的欧盟经济一体化，其实英国享有好处有限，反而欧盟有效的利用了英国资源进行发展，特别是金融行业，英国未加入欧盟前英国是欧洲金融中心，加入后虽说伦敦交易中心还是欧洲金融中心，但是影响力日益下降，欧盟将伦敦金融模式搬到巴黎和法兰克福。形成了当前欧洲三大金融市场。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>　　这点上英国是吃亏的，导致英国金融行业产值下降，虽说还顶着和纽约交易所并称的两个世界最大的金融中心，但是一个在衰退，一个在发展壮大，差距将会越来越大，再加上亚洲的东京、上海、新加坡等金融交易所的发展，与伦敦交易所的差距逐渐缩小，因此英国金融行业在加入欧盟后没有得到应有的发展，反而倒退。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>　　再来说一下对后市金融市场影响</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>　　若英国无协议脱欧，对当前金融市场打击还是有点大的，因英国和欧盟之间商品就需要征收关税，或会引起一定的进口出口恐慌，股市下跌。金融市场的连带效应，或会引起全球股市下跌。英国脱欧进入关键的谈判阶段，而且主要问题聚焦在北爱尔兰关税问题上，如果此次欧盟峰会不能达成共识，英国无协议脱欧风险将会再次加剧，英镑恐怕又要遭受打击。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-46bab4f68b4a65298f6d559a7d88d80f_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2102\" data-rawheight=\"1509\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"2102\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-46bab4f68b4a65298f6d559a7d88d80f_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;2102&#39; height=&#39;1509&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2102\" data-rawheight=\"1509\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"2102\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-46bab4f68b4a65298f6d559a7d88d80f_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-46bab4f68b4a65298f6d559a7d88d80f_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>　　连带的或引起金市的剧烈波动，最新消息称，卢森堡外长称，在峰会达成脱欧协议的可能性非常小。“双重担保”是对于当前僵局实际的解决办法。目前脱欧进展取决于英国，相信有可能在12月前达成脱欧协议。法国财长勒梅尔也表示，我们离达成脱欧协议尚有较远距离，希望在未来数周达成脱欧协议。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>　　若脱欧未取得关键性进展，英国不排除启动“硬脱欧”，随即英镑下跌，黄金或会闻声开涨，还需要注意的一个，就是美元指数。英镑跌，美元指数涨，黄金也涨。这样的行情，跟2016年英国全民公投脱欧之后，英镑，美元，黄金，的整体走势比较相像。这次会不会重演类似剧情呢？就目前黄金整体走势情况来说，还有待商榷。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>　　近期受全球股市大跌以及欧洲政局不定的影响，黄金的避险属性再次显现，金价出现了一波明显的反弹。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>　　不过随着昨日美股和欧股出现了不同程度的反弹，同时意大利政府在最后时刻达成预算协议，降低了政治紧张局势并消除了一段时间以来的一大风险，这使得市场的避险情绪有所消退，黄金再次回落，但是维持在1220美元关键支撑位上方，短时间中性偏多的走势没有发生改变。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>　　此外全球最大的黄金ETF——SPDR上一交易日持仓增加约4.1吨，未连续五天增加，也是五个月以来最长连续增长，这显示出黄金ETF投资者信心出现转，仍有望给金价提供支撑。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>　　今日欧盟峰会召开前，黄金再次出现小幅的反弹，因市场仍然怀疑周三的欧盟峰会能否在北爱尔兰边界问题上取得明显进展，避险情绪小幅回升。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-969466ff27201203a6d7aa09ec2cf3db_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1004\" data-rawheight=\"583\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1004\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-969466ff27201203a6d7aa09ec2cf3db_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;             "title": "李拾雨：10.17昨夜黄金抹平涨幅，黄金空头是回光返照，还是继续称霸", 
            "content": "<p>　　全球股市大跌带来的避险需求、脆弱的美国通胀数据、美元指数走低及技术性买盘大幅启动等，失宠许久的黄金避险属性回归，再度受到市场青睐，资金从风险资产回归黄金，令金价获得支撑突破关键阻力位，从技术来看，黄金多头的涨势将会延续。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-30e389774cfacc609a60f7caccda8f1c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1000\" data-rawheight=\"666\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-30e389774cfacc609a60f7caccda8f1c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1000&#39; height=&#39;666&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1000\" data-rawheight=\"666\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-30e389774cfacc609a60f7caccda8f1c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-30e389774cfacc609a60f7caccda8f1c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>　　美债收益率的息差为100个基点，这一差距在去年12月约为120个基点。息差缩小应该令市场感到紧张，然而长期收益率不断飙升，看似不只受到了美国经济的影响。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>　　美联储仍然会按部就班地实行紧缩政策，美联储将继续加息直到2020年，这是很危险的做法。美联储的紧缩政策令投资者对美国经济的信心大降，在美联储停止加息之前，标普500指数还要跌至2500点的水平，因此劝告投资者不要期待股市能在第四季度实现反弹。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>　　此外，英国脱欧、意大利债务等对黄金影响不容忽视。欧元区英国脱欧分歧犹在，投资者密切关注欧盟峰会，寻找英国脱欧谈判取得突破的信号。同时意大利财政预算仍有风险，如果意大利一意孤行，欧盟的财政规定将变得毫无意义，从而导致其他欧盟成员国纷纷效仿，这对于欧洲央行未来财政政策的实施无疑增加了重重阻碍。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-a2cafa5344e8950f9779de5912b6f21c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1055\" data-rawheight=\"529\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1055\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-a2cafa5344e8950f9779de5912b6f21c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1055&#39; height=&#39;529&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1055\" data-rawheight=\"529\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1055\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-a2cafa5344e8950f9779de5912b6f21c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-a2cafa5344e8950f9779de5912b6f21c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>　　种种原因归结到一起，拾雨个人认为后市黄金大趋势任然看涨，这归于投资者对目前美国经济的不信任，股市动荡，美债风险加大等等影响美元霸权地位，美元代替比了黄金避险，导致避险资本涌入黄金交易市场，再加上年底实物黄金需求增加，也是一个推动金价上涨的因素。截止发稿，金价回落到1223.4附近，是黄金空头继续称霸，还是回光返照？</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>　　拾雨个人看法是黄金空头回光返照，在多头力量爆发后的垂死挣扎，指望压制多头，但是就目前全球金融市场乱象来看，避险资本的涌入很好的提振金价，因此后市黄金看涨思路不变，月底之前可看到1268阻力位附近。因此目前来说是中长线多单布局的好机会。至于具体布局方案拾雨会在实盘中给出。至于日内操作，拾雨建议低多为主，高空为辅。1224附近可做多，目标1240，破位则可继续持仓；若与反弹，则平仓多单，空单进场。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-38ad32de983e22e48213c7be0e6d2cb4_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"900\" data-rawheight=\"542\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"900\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-38ad32de983e22e48213c7be0e6d2cb4_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;900&#39; height=&#39;542&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"900\" data-rawheight=\"542\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"900\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-38ad32de983e22e48213c7be0e6d2cb4_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-38ad32de983e22e48213c7be0e6d2cb4_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>　　本文由李拾雨撰写，以上内容供参考，只代表拾雨个人观点，投资有风险，入市需谨慎，行情瞬息万变，文章时效性强，具有滞后性。具体操作以实盘为准。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>　　谢谢阅读！</p>",

            "title": "第281期：jubilee和anniversary", 
            "content": "<p>今天我们来学一个新词，jubilee，意思是“周年庆”、“大庆”，你知道jubilee和anniversary有什么区别吗？</p><p>先来看英文释义：</p><p>Ajubileeis a particularanniversaryof an event, usually denoting the 25th, 50th, 60th, or 70th anniversary.</p><p>韦伯斯特字典的解释最精当：a jubilee is a special anniversary especially:a 50th anniversary（特别指50周年大庆）</p><p>简单地说，anniversary表示任何一个整数年份的周年庆，例如什么什么三周年，而且有一个确切的日期，只是周年纪念，不一定有庆典活动。</p><p>而jubilee指的是主要年份的anniversary时举行的庆典，不一定对应那个确切的日期，可以是整年。例如：The  Queen of England will be celebrating her Diamond Jubilee this year,  marking 60 years on the throne. 英国女王在位60周年钻石大庆（2012年）</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-fe40b4b9bd4f0128395ddd715417f07f_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"355\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-fe40b4b9bd4f0128395ddd715417f07f_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;355&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"355\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-fe40b4b9bd4f0128395ddd715417f07f_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-fe40b4b9bd4f0128395ddd715417f07f_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>英国女王的这种庆典就叫public jubilee了。A public Jubilee is a ceremony that celebrates an anniversary.</p><p>下面是几个最常用的jubilee year的英文说法：</p><p>Celebrations in the reign of a monarch: （庆祝某君王在位时用）</p><ul><li>Silver jubilee, for a 25th anniversary 25周年叫银庆<br/> </li><li>Ruby jubilee, for a 40th anniversary 40周年叫红宝石庆<br/> </li><li>Golden jubilee, for a 50th anniversary 50周年叫金庆<br/> </li><li>Diamond jubilee, for a 60th anniversary 60周年叫钻石庆<br/> </li><li>Platinum jubilee, for a 70th anniversary 70周年叫铂金庆</li></ul><p>看一个大家容易理解的例句：<br/>The Chinese people celebrated the golden <i>jubilee</i> of the founding of their People&#39;s Republic on October 1st,1999.</p><p>是不是觉得耳熟？想起了“金婚”、“钻石婚”？下面总结一下所有年份婚姻庆典的英文名称。</p><ul><li>One (1) year – Cotton Jubilee</li><li>Two (2) years – Paper Jubilee</li><li>Three (3) years – Leather Jubilee</li><li>Four (4) years – Flower/Fruit Jubilee</li><li>Five (5) years – Wooden Jubilee</li><li>Six (6) years – Iron Jubilee</li><li>Seven (7) years – Wool</li><li>Eight (8) years – Bronze Jubilee</li><li>Nine (9) years – Copper Jubilee</li><li>Ten (10) years – Tin/Aluminium Jubilee</li><li>Eleven (11) years – Steel Jubilee</li><li>Twelve (12) years – Silk and Fine Linen Jubilee</li><li>Thirteen (13) years – Lace Jubilee</li><li>Fourteen (14) years – Ivory Jubilee</li><li>Fifteen (15) years – Crystal Jubilee</li><li>Twenty (20) years – China/Porcelain Jubilee</li><li>Twenty Five (25) years – Silver Jubilee</li><li>Thirty (30) years – Pearl Jubilee</li><li>Thirty Five (35) years – Coral Jubilee</li><li>Forty (40) years – Ruby Jubilee</li><li>Forty Five (45) years – Sapphire</li><li>Fifty (50) years – Golden Jubilee</li><li>Fifty Five (55) years – Emerald Jubilee</li><li>Sixty (60) years – Diamond Jubilee</li></ul><p>最后，一个小重点请注意，jubilee的发音不要搞错，重音在最后一个音节lee上。<br/>今天先讲这么多吧。其实jubilee这个词还可以讲很多内容，历史、来源、犹太人的传统、在圣经中的故事等等。限于篇幅，本文就讲到这里。</p><p>*原文发布于：</p><a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//giraffenglish.net/2018/10/16/jubilee-and-anniversary/\" data-draft-node=\"block\" data-draft-type=\"link-card\" noreferrer\">第281期：jubilee和anniversary - 長頸鹿英語</a><p></p>",

            "url": "https://zhuanlan.zhihu.com/p/46854611", 
            "userName": "高翻考研经济学人", 
            "userLink": "https://www.zhihu.com/people/bb6ed77ba91df2511411450f2ac2fd20", 
            "upvote": 1, 
            "title": "经济学人双语精读| The next recession", 
            "content": "<p>经济学人五期招新/ 倒计时啦，赶快上车了啦。</p><p>请参考公众号</p><p><a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//weixin.qq.com/r/lS0XD4TEAdl_rcBs93iH\" class=\" external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\"><span class=\"invisible\">http://</span><span class=\"visible\">weixin.qq.com/r/lS0XD4T</span><span class=\"invisible\">EAdl_rcBs93iH</span><span class=\"ellipsis\"></span></a> (二维码自动识别)</p><p>20181013 Leader 板块  ，译文为参考译文</p><p>The world economy </p><p>The next recession </p><p>JUST a year ago the world was enjoying a synchronised economic acceleration. In 2017 growth rose in every big advanced economy except Britain, and in most emerging ones. Global trade was surging and America booming; China’s slide into deflation had been quelled; even the euro zone was thriving. In 2018 the story is very different. This week stockmarkets tumbled across the globe as investors worried, for the second time this year, about slowing growth and the effects of tighter American monetary policy. Those fears are well-founded. </p><p>The world economy’s problem in 2018 has been uneven momentum. In America President Donald Trump’s tax cuts have helped lift annualised quarterly growth above 4%. Unemployment is at its lowest since 1969. Yet the IMF thinks growth will slow this year in every other big advanced economy. And emerging markets are in trouble. </p><p>This divergence between America and the rest means divergent monetary policies, too. The Federal Reserve has raised interest rates eight times since December 2015. The European Central Bank (ECB) is still a long way from its first increase. In Japan rates are negative. China, the principal target of Mr Trump’s trade war, relaxed monetary policy this week in response to a weakening economy. When interest rates rise in America but nowhere else, the dollar strengthens. That makes it harder for emerging markets to repay their dollar debts. A rising greenback has already helped propel Argentina and Turkey into trouble; this week Pakistan asked the IMF for a bail-out. </p><p>Emerging markets account for 59% of the world’s output (measured by purchasing power), up from 43% just two decades ago, when the Asian financial crisis hit. Their problems could soon wash back onto America’s shores, just as Uncle Sam’s domestic boom starts to peter out. The rest of the world could be in a worse state by then, too, if Italy’s budget difficulties do not abate or China suffers a sharp slowdown. </p><p>Cutting-room floors </p><p>The good news is that banking systems are more resilient than a decade ago, when the crisis struck. The chance of a downturn as severe as the one that struck then is low. Emerging markets are inflicting losses on investors, but in the main their real economies seem to be holding up. The trade war has yet to cause serious harm, even in China. If America’s boom gives way to a shallow recession as fiscal stimulus diminishes and rates rise, that would not be unusual after a decade of growth. </p><p>Yet this is where the bad news comes in. As our special report this week sets out, the rich world in particular is ill-prepared to deal with even a mild recession. That is partly because the policy arsenal is still depleted from fighting the last downturn. In the past half-century, the Fed has typically cut interest rates by five or so percentage points in a downturn. Today it has less than half that room before it reaches zero; the euro zone and Japan have no room at all. </p><p>Policymakers have other options, of course. Central banks could use the now-familiar policy of quantitative easing (QE), the purchase of securities with newly created central-bank reserves. The efficacy of QE is debated, but if that does not work, they could try more radical, untested approaches, such as giving money directly to individuals. Governments can boost spending, too. Even countries with large debt burdens can benefit from fiscal stimulus during recessions. </p><p>The question is whether using these weapons is politically acceptable. Central banks will enter the next recession with balance-sheets that are already swollen by historical standards—the Fed’s is worth 20% of GDP. Opponents of QE say that it distorts markets and inflates asset bubbles, among other things. No matter that these views are largely misguided; fresh bouts of QE would attract even closer scrutiny than last time. The constraints are particularly tight in the euro zone, where the ECB is limited to buying 33% of any country’s public debt. </p><p>Spending ceilings </p><p>Fiscal stimulus would also attract political opposition, regardless of the economic arguments. The euro zone is again the most worrying case, if only because Germans and other northern Europeans fear that they will be left with unpaid debts if a country defaults. Its restrictions on borrowing are designed to restrain profligacy, but they also curb the potential for stimulus. America is more willing to spend, but it has recently increased its deficit to over 4% of GDP with the economy already running hot. If it needs to widen the deficit still further to counter a recession, expect a political fight. </p><p>Politics is an even greater obstacle to international action. Unprecedented cross-border co-operation was needed to fend off the crisis in 2008. But the rise of populists will complicate the task of working together. The Fed’s swap lines with other central banks, which let them borrow dollars from America, might be a flashpoint. And falling currencies may feed trade tensions. This week Steve Mnuchin, the treasury secretary, warned China against “competitive devaluations”. Mr Trump’s belief in the harm caused by trade deficits is mistaken when growth is strong. But when demand is short, protectionism is a more tempting way to stimulate the economy. </p><p>Timely action could avert some of these dangers. Central banks could have new targets that make it harder to oppose action during and after a crisis. If they established a commitment ahead of time to make up lost ground when inflation undershoots or growth disappoints, expectations of a catch-up boom could provide an automatic stimulus in any downturn. Alternatively, raising the inflation target today could over time push up interest rates, giving more room for rate cuts. Future fiscal stimulus could be baked in now by increasing the potency of “automatic stabilisers”—spending on unemployment insurance, say, which goes up as economies sag. The euro zone could relax its fiscal rules to allow for more stimulus. </p><p>Pre-emptive action calls for initiative from politicians, which is conspicuously absent. This week’s market volatility suggests time could be short. The world should start preparing now for the next recession, while it still can.■</p><p>The next recession 世界下一个经济大萧条</p><p>When the downturn comes, toxic politics and constrained central banks will add to the risk </p><p>全球经济衰退来临时，政治上的乌烟瘴气和央行的捉襟见肘，让风险增大</p><p>■When the downturn comes 我们还可以说 when the downturn strikes/ hits</p><p>  Downturn in sth   (商业经济的)衰退,下降,衰退期:</p><p>  a downturn in sales / trade / business </p><p> 销量/贸易/营业额下降 </p><p>  the economic downturn of the late 1990s </p><p>   20 世纪 90 年代末的经济衰退 </p><p>■reces·sion  /noun C,U</p><p>1. 〔经济〕衰退，萧条:</p><p>•There is deep recession in the UK.英国处于严重的经济衰退之中。</p><p>into / out of recession</p><p>•attempts to pull the country out of recession推动国家走出经济衰退期的努力</p><p>Just a year ago the world was enjoying a syncronised economic acceleraton. In 2017 growth rose in every big advanced economy except Britain, and in most emerging ones. Global trade was surging and America booming; China&#39;s slide into deflation had been quelled(缓解);even the euro zone was thriving. In 2018 the story is very different. This week stockmarkets tumbled across the globe as investors worried, for the second time this year, about slowing growth and the effects of  tighter American monetary policy. Those fears are well-founded. </p><p>一年前，世界经济同步增速。2017年，除英国增速放缓外，所有发达国家和大部分新兴国家的经济都呈现增长态势。全球贸易陡增，美国经济繁荣。中国通货紧缩趋势得以缓解，甚至欧元区经济也蓬勃发展。2018年，经济情况却天差地别。本周，全球股市大震荡，投资者纷纷担心受经济放缓和美联储持续收紧的货币政策影响，担心股指二次探底。这些担忧是有理有据的。</p><p>【小词活用】</p><p>■enjoy 拥有; 享有 外刊高频词汇</p><p>【经济学人】It’s possible Europe might enjoy a few short-term benefits as China and the United States duke it out. If, for example, China were to raise tariffs on Boeing airliners, Boeing’s European rival, Airbus, could take advantage. But positive effects of that sort are not likely to outweigh the risks.</p><p>【2017政府工作报告】We will promote workmanship and foster a culture of workmanship where workers have a strong ethic and tirelessly seek improvement. We will see great numbers of Chinese workers exemplify workmanship and more Chinese brands enjoy international recognition. We will usher in an era of quality for economic development in China.要大力弘扬工匠精神，厚植工匠文化，恪尽职业操守，崇尚精益求精，培育众多“中国工匠”，打造更多享誉世界的“中国品牌”，推动中国经济发展进入质量时代。</p><p>■acceleration /noun</p><p>1. 加快，增速:</p><p>[+ in ]</p><p>•an acceleration in the rate of inflation通货膨胀率的加快</p><p>[+ of ]</p><p>•the rapid acceleration of economic progress in South East Asia东南亚经济的快速增长</p><p>■boom noun | verb</p><p> 1 boom / bum ; bu:m /noun</p><p>1. INCREASE IN BUSINESS 业务增加, sing.a quick increase of business activity〔生意〕繁荣，兴旺，激增; 同义词 ：slump</p><p>•The boom has created job opportunities.经济繁荣创造了就业的机会。</p><p>[+ in ]</p><p>•a sudden boom in the housing market房产市场的突然兴旺</p><p>consumer / investment / property etc boom</p><p>•the post-war property boom战后财富的迅速增长</p><p>boom years / times</p><p>•In boom times, airlines do well.在经济繁荣时期，航空公司生意很好。</p><p>•the economic boom of the 1950s  20 世纪 50 年代的经济繁荣</p><p>•The economy went from boom to bustvery quickly.经济很快就从繁荣走向了萧条。</p><p>2. 流行，风靡:</p><p>•the disco boom of the 1970s 20 世纪 70 年代的迪斯科热</p><p>[+ in ]</p><p>•the boom in youth soccer in the U.S.美国的青年足球热</p><p>3. 隆隆声</p><p>⇒sonic boom</p><p>4. 帆桁，帆杆</p><p> boom /verb</p><p>1. 〔商业、贸易等〕繁荣，迅速发展:</p><p>•Business was booming , and money wasn&#39;t a problem.生意非常兴隆，钱已不是问题。</p><p>2. also boom (sth ↔ ) out 用洪亮而低沉的声音说:</p><p>•&#39;Ladies and gentlemen,&#39; his voice boomed out.“女士们，先生们。”他的声音低沉而有力。</p><p>3. also boom out Ito make a loud deep sound发出低沉的声音，隆隆作响:</p><p>•Guns boomed in the distance.远处大炮隆隆作响。</p><p>—booming adj:</p><p>•a booming economy迅速发展的经济</p><p>近义词spring up, roar ahead, boom, thrive, blossom, prosper</p><p>■surge verb | noun</p><p> surge //verb </p><p>1. 迅速涌动，蜂拥向前:</p><p>[+ forward / through etc ]</p><p>•The crowd surged through the gates.人群蜂拥着通过大门。</p><p>2. 〔情感〕涌起，涌现:</p><p>•She could feel anger surging inside her.她感到自己怒火中烧。</p><p>3. 〔大量液体〕汹涌;〔电流〕浪涌;〔化学品等〕突然涌动:</p><p>•A wave surged up towards them.一个浪头向他们涌来。</p><p>4.突然上涨，激增;=shoot up</p><p>•Oil prices surged.油价暴涨。</p><p> 2 </p><p>Surge /noun </p><p>1. 〔情感的〕突发; 涌现:</p><p>•a surge of excitement一阵兴奋</p><p>2. a sudden increase in amount or number〔数量的〕急剧增加:</p><p>[+ in / of ]</p><p>•a surge in food costs食品成本的急剧增加</p><p>3. a sudden movement of a lot of people〔人群的〕蜂拥:</p><p>[+ of ]</p><p>•a surge of refugees into the country涌入这个国家的难民</p><p>4.〔液体的〕汹涌;〔电流的〕浪涌;〔化学品等的〕突然涌动:</p><p>•a device that protects your computer against electrical surges一台计算机电涌保护设备</p><p>Tumble </p><p>■tumble verb | noun</p><p> tumble  /verb </p><p>1. 倒下，跌倒，摔倒; 滚下，翻滚下来:</p><p>[+ over / backwards / down ]</p><p>•A few stones came tumbling down the cliff.几块石头从悬崖上滚落下来。</p><p>2. always + adv / prepto move in an uncontrolled way莽莽撞撞地行动; 胡乱地走:</p><p>[+ into / through / out etc ]</p><p>•We tumbled out into the street.我们跌跌撞撞地出来，到了大街上。</p><p>3.〔价格或数字〕猛跌，暴跌:</p><p>•Oil prices have tumbled.石油价格猛跌。</p><p>[+ to ]</p><p>•Mortgage rates tumbled to their lowest level for 25 years.按揭贷款利率一下子跌到了 25 年来的最低水平点。</p><p>4.〔长而鬈曲的浓密头发〕垂下，垂落:</p><p>•Her long dark hair tumbled over her shoulders.她那深色的长发垂落在肩头。</p><p>5. 〔因兴奋或伤心而〕快速说:</p><p>[+ out / over ]</p><p>•The words tumbled out as if he hardly knew what to say first.他语无伦次的，好像不知道先说什么才好。</p><p>6.〔水〕快速流动:</p><p>•A narrow stream tumbled over the rocks.一条狭窄的小溪从岩石上滚滚流过。</p><p> 2 </p><p>Tumble /noun </p><p>1. a fall, especially from a high place or level〔尤指从高处〕倒下，跌倒，摔倒:</p><p>•It&#39;s possible that stocks could take a tumble next year.明年股票有可能会暴跌。</p><p>⇒rough and tumble激烈的竞争；混战</p><p>【知识小结】表示“下降、减少” 有哪些词汇？建议用每个单词仿写个句子</p><p>一般词汇：decline, decrease, reduce， dip (减少，降低), fall</p><p>高级词汇：plummet（暴跌），plunge（暴跌，骤降），slide（逐渐降低），dwindle（逐渐缩小、减少），tumble（暴跌，骤降），sink（减少，减弱），slump（锐减，猛跌）</p><p>【China Daily】The Shanghai Composite Index sank 6.4 percent to 2749.79,marking its lowest close since December 2014, while the Shenzhen Component Index slumped 7 percent to close at 9483.55.</p><p>上证综合指数下跌6.4%至2749.79，是自2014年12月以来最低收市水平。与此同时，深成指也下跌达7%，收盘为9483.55.</p><p>■well founded  adjective   理由充足的；有根据的；有事实依据的 反义词：ill-founded（ 凭空的；无根据的；毫无理由的:）</p><p>  His fear turned out to be well founded. </p><p> 他的恐惧证明是有道理的。 </p><p> All our fears proved ill-founded. </p><p> 我们所有的担心结果都证明是杞人忧天。</p>",

            "upvote": 0, 
            "title": "第280期：shortchange", 
            "content": "<p>我们都知道买东西时被商家多收了钱叫overcharge, 今天我们来学一下被商家少找了钱的说法：shortchange.</p><p>这个词其实很简单，change就是零钱、找零的意思。shortchange（连起来写）就是被少找了零钱。用英语解释就是：to give someone back less money than they are owed when the person is buying something from you.</p><p>（韦伯斯特大辞典）例句：</p><p>The cashier <i>shortchanged</i>  me. I gave her 10 dollars to pay for an $8.95 book, and she only gave  me a dollar back. 收银员少找钱了。我买了本定价8.95美元的书，给了她10美元，她只找了我一美元。 </p><p>这个意思很好理解，也很容易记住。但是佛老建议你联想扩充一下shortchange的同义词、近义词。 Shortchange的近义词非常多，请大家自行学习。下面仅举几个例子以作大家自学的线索。 </p><p>beat, bilk, bleed, cheat, chisel, con, cozen, defraud, do, do in, fiddle, fleece, flimflam, gaff, gyp, hustle, mulct, pluck, ream, rip off, rook, screw, shake down, short, skin, squeeze, stick, stiff, sting, swindle, victimize</p><p>（不知道谁有兴趣把上面这些shortchange的近义词逐个查一下字典。说实话，有好几个佛老也不认识。）</p><p>好了，我们接着来学习shortchange的第二层意思。</p><p>在基础意思“被少找钱”的意思上，shortchange的引申含义是：to treat someone unfairly, by giving them less than they deserve. </p><p>这个意思怎么理解呢？大意就是“不恰当地对待某人”，或”给某人与其实力和地位不相称的待遇“、“对......不公平”。大家应该不难从shortchange少找零这个意思联想到这一层意思。 </p><p>来看一个新鲜的例句： </p><p>The trade war was triggered by the Trump administration, which argues that existing trade relationships  <i><b><u>shortchange</u></b></i> U.S. industry. 这轮贸易战由川普政府发起，理由是现有的贸易关系对美国的工业造成了<b><u>不公。</u></b> </p><p>怎么样，这个词很传神吧？</p><p>继续来看，to shortchange is to give someone or something less money, time, or attention than is deserved. 你可以把这个解释看作shortchange的第三层意思，也可以看作是上面第二层意思的另一个解释。 </p><p>例句： </p><p> The singer <i>shortchanged</i> his fans by singing for only 30 minutes.  那个歌手只唱了30分钟，亏欠了歌迷。 </p><p>可能那个歌手演唱会原本计划唱2个小时的，结果只唱了半个小时，对歌迷构成了亏欠和欺骗。 </p><p>你看这里的shortchange多传神。 </p><p>大家学会用shortchange了吗？ </p><p>佛老希望每天的这个原创系列小文不辜负近千名读者的期望，不浪费大家的时间。Folao will never shortchange his readers. </p><p>最后，我们来看一句欧巴马总统的名言，大家试着翻译一下。欢迎留言分享你的翻译。 </p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-1670060fd0a6795430e54bf3c7474820_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"864\" data-rawheight=\"612\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"864\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-1670060fd0a6795430e54bf3c7474820_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;             "title": "第279期：143 and 1432", 
            "content": "<p>如果有个外国朋友给你发手机短信说“143”，你知道是什么意思吗？</p><p>今天我们来学一些歪果仁常用的手机短信和网络聊天用语的缩写形式。这些词叫internet acronym，也叫internet slang.</p><p><u>答案公布</u> </p><p>143 = I love you.</p><p>因为：1,  4, and 3 are the number of letters in the corresponding word.  因为I是一个字母，love有4个字母，you有3个字母。英语中就用143这三个数字来简写I love  you这句话了。（只用在手机短信、即时聊天、网络聊天等场景中，正式文书和场合慎用）</p><p>例如：</p><p>I have 2 go. 143.</p><p>这句短信的完整形式是：I have to go. I love you. （多用于情侣之间）</p><p>如果对方回复，通常会这样写：1432. 什么意思？不难猜出来是I love you too吧。2在英语短信中一般都是too到简写形式。</p><p>其实说到这里，大家应该觉得不陌生。因为汉语中也有很多类似的简写、缩略写法。例如“我爱你”可以写作520，“一生一世”写作1314等等。</p><p>佛老记得很多年前在雅虎聊天室跟一个美国网友聊天，他忽然打了句&#34;TTYL&#34;，然后就下线了。当时我还没明白，后来才知道TTYL就是Talk to you later. 是“再见”、“回聊”的意思。那是十几年前的事了，这个缩写我就一直记得。</p><p>下面，我们来看一些常用的英语缩略写法，方便大家在和外国朋友手机聊天时快速打字并看懂对方的意思。</p><p>abt - about</p><p>2 - two, too</p><p>ayt - alright (例句：r u feeling ayt? -- Are you feeling alright?)</p><p>b4 - before</p><p>bb - baby</p><p>bbl - be back later (离开一下，一会儿回来）</p><p>brb - be right back（马上回来）</p><p>brt - be right there （马上到）</p><p>b/c - because</p><p>bff - best friend forever （一辈子的好兄弟/朋友。bff本来只是用在网络聊天中的一个缩写，后来成了很多人口语中常说的单词）</p><p>esad - eat shit and die （吃屎去死）类似的还有foad（fxxk off and die)</p><p>omg - oh my God（中国的网络语中有一句“哦卖糕的，是不是蒸的？- oh my God. Really? 佛老特别喜欢这句:)</p><p>h8 - hate （例如：I h8 u. - I hate you.）有时候也写作h8t.</p><p>hbu - how about you?</p><p>idk - i don&#39;t know/i don&#39;t care</p><p>还有很多很多这样的缩写。大多是约定俗成的写法，不能自己独创。大家平日可多多留意，不断总结。佛老还会专文整理总结这个小专题，敬请留意。</p><p>Ok, got 2 go. lunch time. </p><p>参考链接：<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//www.smart-words.org/abbreviations/text.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">50 Popular Internet Acronyms</a></p><p>*原文发布于：</p><a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//giraffenglish.net/2018/10/14/143-and-1432/\" data-draft-node=\"block\" data-draft-type=\"link-card\" data-image=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-1d70a7df044e930dff0478d38c8d8f4e_180x120.jpg\" data-image-width=\"670\" data-image-height=\"335\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">第279期：143 and 1432 - 長頸鹿英語</a><p></p>",

            "title": "经济学人双语精读| Gig economy", 
            "content": "<p>经济学人双语精读第五期招新啦，喊你来学习啦，小伙伴们快上车啦</p><p>更多请浏览公众号</p><p><a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//weixin.qq.com/r/lS0XD4TEAdl_rcBs93iH\" class=\" external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\"><span class=\"invisible\">http://</span><span class=\"visible\">weixin.qq.com/r/lS0XD4T</span><span class=\"invisible\">EAdl_rcBs93iH</span><span class=\"ellipsis\"></span></a> (二维码自动识别)</p><p>本文选自经济学人20181006 期Leader 板块</p><p>Workers on tap </p><p>How governments should deal with the rise of the gig economy</p><p>Watch it by all means, but welcome it </p><p><b>■on tap</b> [固定表达] 可随时使用的(available to be used at any time) </p><p>We have this sort of information on tap. 我们可随时向您提供这种资料。</p><p>招之即来的工人</p><p>政府该如何应对零工经济</p><p>务必监管，但也开诚接纳</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-34ad5728db54279cecc78a40e1bafadf_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"560\" data-rawheight=\"361\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"560\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-34ad5728db54279cecc78a40e1bafadf_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;560&#39; height=&#39;361&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"560\" data-rawheight=\"361\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"560\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-34ad5728db54279cecc78a40e1bafadf_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-34ad5728db54279cecc78a40e1bafadf_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>THE Archbishop of Canterbury sees it as “the reincarnation of an ancient evil”. Elizabeth Warren, a senator from Massachusetts, says that, for many workers, it is the “next step in a losing effort to build some economic security in a world where all the benefits are floating to the top 10%”. Luigi Di Maio, Italy’s deputy prime minister, is going after it as part of his “war on precarious work”.</p><p>坎特伯雷大主教把零工经济看作是“一个远古邪灵的化身”。马萨诸塞州参议员伊丽莎白•沃伦(Elizabeth Warren)表示，对于许多工人来说，零工经济提供的经济保障将前功尽弃，因为10%的高层人员摄取了零工经济带来的所有利益。意大利副总理路易吉•迪•马约(Luigi Di Maio)正在深究此事，作为他“向不稳定工作开战”的一部分。</p><p><b>Para 1 引入话题：坎特伯雷大主教 和马萨诸塞州参议员的评述做铺垫引出零工经济负面话题。接着说了意大利政府应对零工经济。</b></p><p><b>■reincarnation</b>   [ˌri:ɪnkɑ:ˈneɪʃn] n. a person or an animal whose body contains the soul of a dead person （灵魂的）转世化身，化身</p><p>[TED 演讲]I don&#39;t know if I can change the world yet, &#39;cause I don&#39;t know that much about it, and I don&#39;t know that much about reincarnation either, but if you make me laugh hard enough, sometimes I forget what century I&#39;m in.</p><p>我还不知道我是否能改变这世界， 因为我处世不深-- 同时我关于转世也了解得不多， 但假若你使我开怀大笑， 有时我会忘了我所处的世纪。</p><p><b>■precarious</b>  /adjective</p><p>1. 〔局势或状态〕不稳定的，不安全的，危险的:</p><p>•Her health remained precarious, despite the treatment.尽管接受了治疗，她的健康状况还是不稳定。</p><p>•the company&#39;s precarious financial position 公司岌岌可危的财务状况</p><p>2. 可能倒的，不稳的，不牢靠的:</p><p>•a precarious mountain trail危险的山间小路</p><p>—precariously adv:</p><p>•a cup of tea balanced precariously on her knee她膝盖上晃晃悠悠放着的一杯茶</p><p>—precariousness noun U</p><p>· [长难句理解] Elizabeth Warren, a senator from Massachusetts, says that, for many workers, it is the “next step in a losing effort to build some economic security in a world where all the benefits are floating to the top 10%”. 首先用了一个同位语去修饰这个人，我们在写作中也要习惯用同位语。这里从句的写法很有意思，我们可以试着理解字里行间的讽刺意味。零工经济最初的目的是为了提供经济保障(build some economic security)，可作者在前面用了in a losing effort to，表明了作者的立场，他认为零工经济不仅没能提供经济保障，还使人们丧失了经济保障。</p><p>[背景了解] 坎特伯雷大主教(Archbishop of Canterbury)，又称为坎特伯雷圣座(the See of Canterbury)，首任主教是圣奥斯定·坎特伯雷，为全英格兰的首席主教(The Primate of All England)。坎特伯雷大主教的权威，不但是承受了他的历史事实，更是在天主教会中的圣礼事保持者。他是全英国教会的主教长(The See of Church of England)，又是全世界圣公会的主教长(The Patriarch of the Anglican Communion of Churches)，普世圣公宗精神领袖(Leader of the Anglican Communion)，主持自1867年起的每十年一次的全世界圣公会主教会议。</p><p>Gig economy(零工经济)意指由工作量不多的自由职业者构成的经济领域,他们会利用网站或应用程序快速匹配供需方,在网站上应聘小时工、出租房间、出售手工制品、或出租私家车获得额外收入。一些退休人员和全职主妇也发挥特长打起零工。</p><p>2. For many, the “gig economy”, in which short-term jobs are assigned via online platforms, is a potent symbol of how modern capitalism has failed. Critics rail that it allows firms to rid themselves of well-paid employees, replacing them with cheap freelancers. Workers who once relied on an employer to pay into their pension, or to cover their health care when they fell ill, must instead save for the future themselves. On this reading, the gig economy turbocharges insecurity and the erosion of workers’ hard-won rights. There is a grain of truth to this. But it misses the bigger picture.</p><p>对于很多人来说，“零工经济”-通过网络平台分配短期工作-这是现代资本主义没落的一个有力象征。批评人士指责说，零工经济可以用廉价的自由职业者取代高薪雇员。那些曾靠老板来支付养老金或者医疗保险的工人，现在需要自己为未来储蓄了。由此看来，零工经济增加了不安全因素，侵蚀了工人来之不易的权益。这种说法是有一定道理的，但并没着眼全局。</p><p><b>Para 2 本段论述了零工经济的负面影响，最后一句笔锋一转，指出这种说法有道理但缺乏宏观审度。</b></p><p><b>■assign</b> //verb T</p><p>1. 分配，分派，指派〔任务〕:</p><p>assign sb a task / role</p><p>•I&#39;ve been assigned the task of looking after the new students.指派给我的工作是照料新来的学生。</p><p>assign sb to sth</p><p>•Jan&#39;s been assigned to the Asian Affairs Bureau.简被派到亚洲事务部。</p><p>assign sb to do sth</p><p>•Madison was assigned to investigate a balloon accident.麦迪逊被派去调查一宗气球事故。</p><p>assign sb sth</p><p>•Assign each student a partner.给每个学生分派一个同伴。</p><p>2.确定〔时间、价值、地点等〕:</p><p>•How much time have you assigned for the meeting?你给这个会定了多长时间？</p><p>3. 分配，分派〔钱、设备等〕:</p><p>assign sth to sb</p><p>•A personal bodyguard had been assigned to her.已给她派了一个私人保镖。</p><p>assign sb sth</p><p>•They assigned me a small room.他们分配给我一个小房间。</p><p><b>■【熟词僻义】rail</b> v. (formal) to complain about sth/sb in a very angry way 怒斥；抱怨</p><p><b>■potent /</b> /adjective</p><p>1. 有效力的，效力大的; 有影响力的; 同义词 powerful</p><p>•a potent symbol of oppression压迫的有力象征</p><p>•Advertising is a potent force in showing smoking as a socially acceptable habit.广告有一股强大的力量，显示吸烟是为社会所接受的习惯。</p><p>•A good company pension scheme remains a potent weapon for attracting staff.良好的公司养老金计划依然是吸引员工的有效武器。</p><p>2.强有力的，有威力的:</p><p>•The treaty requires them to get rid of their most potent weapons.条约要求他们销毁威力最强大的武器。</p><p><b>■rid</b> v. 要注意这个词除了大家熟知的get rid of…这一用法外，还有rid sb/sth of sb/sth（去除，清除）这一用法</p><p>【拓展】get rid of sb / sth 丢弃某物; 毁掉某物:</p><p>· [长难句理解] Workers who once relied on an employer to pay into their pension, or to cover their health care when they fell ill, must instead save for the future themselves. 这里who引导限制性定语从句，修饰前面的workers，定语从句中又用了两个并列的to do结构作rely on的间接宾语，详述了员工依赖雇主为他们做什么，must向后才是句子的主干部分，讲述员工未来需要自己存钱支付医疗保险等费用。</p><p><b>■on this reading</b>这里的reading不是简单的指“阅读（活动）”，而是“理解（方法）（the particular way in which you understand a book, situation, etc.）”的意思，因此这个短语有“in this regard（从这方面来说）”的意思。这个词组也可以放到句中，《经济学人》就出现过这样一句话Freud, on this reading, was right about the importance of early experience on character formation. 弗洛伊德认为早期经历对人格发展有重要影响，由此看来这一说法是正确的。</p><p><b>■a grain of truth</b> 一丝真理，一点真实性 [固定搭配]</p><p>Our observations may contain a grain of truth for you to refer to.</p><p>我们的意见也许会有千虑一得之处， 供你参考。</p><p><b>■the bigger picture</b>是英文中的一个常用表达，“最重要的部分，全局”的意思。比如经济学人关于TPP（Trans-Pacific Partnership Agreement跨太平洋伙伴关系协定）的一篇文章中写道But those who believe in free trade, and the benefits it brings, ought not to miss the bigger picture. 但是，信奉自由贸易及其益处的人们不应忽略大环境。我们在写作中，要想表达“全局”这一概念时，就可以使用这一表达。</p><p>3.For one thing, despite city streets clogged with Uber drivers and Deliveroo cyclists, gigging is not about to take over the world (see article). Across the OECD club of mostly rich countries, the share of workers in full-time positions, which dropped after the financial crisis of 2008-09, has been rising. In America the average job tenure has barely changed in the past 30 years. Depending on whom you ask, 1-5% of Americans gig（ 尤指临时的工作）—but many of those have salaried（领薪水的） jobs as well.</p><p>首先，尽管优步（Uber）司机和送餐服务公司Deliveroo外卖小哥在城市街道上随处可见，但零工经济并不会主宰世界。自2008年至2009年的经济危机后，在经合组织(OECD)大多数富裕成员国中，全职工作人员的比例所有下降，而现在一直稳步上升。在过去三十年间，美国平均工作年限几乎没有任何改变。根据调查对象不同，约1%到5%的美国人是零时工，但他们中的许多人都有带薪的正式工作。</p><p> ■for &#39;one thing   (用以引出两个以上的理由之一)一来,一方面:</p><p> &#39;Why don&#39;t you get a car?&#39; &#39;Well, for one thing, I can&#39;t drive!&#39; </p><p>   &#34;你为什么不买辆汽车呢？&#34; &#34;啊,首先,我不会开车！&#34; </p><p> ■clog up with sth | ~ sth (up) (with sth)(使)阻塞,堵塞</p><p> •Over many years, the pipes had got clogged up with grease.多年下来管道都被油腻物堵塞了。</p><p>【经济学人】On Diwali and ten succeeding days this year, Delhi’s air was clogged with averages of well over 500µg/m³, with peaks of up to 1,000µg/m³.</p><p>今年光明节及节后的十日内，新德里的PM2.5指数平均值远超500微克/立方米，最高值达到1000微克/立方米，导致空气停滞不通。</p><p>■ take over 接管; 接任; 接手;</p><p>•His only reason for investing in the company was to take it over.他投资这家公司唯一的原因是想接管它。</p><p>Takeover 收购；接收；接管:</p><p>•Thornbury has announced a takeover bid of a regional TV company.索恩伯里已经宣布将出价收购一家区域性电视公司。</p><p>[卫报]Last year, the BBC invited two Chinese teachers to take over a sixth-form class in the documentary Are Our Kids Tough Enough? (Spoiler: they weren’t, but nor were the teachers.)</p><p>[词语拓展] at the helm, take the helm</p><p>[经济学人]Since taking the helm in 2011 Stuart Gulliver has reversed the empire-building that took place in the 2000s to refocus the bank on financing trade.</p><p>欧智华自2011年开始掌控汇丰银行以来，修正了汇丰银行在21世纪初的金融帝国打造途径，以重新将重心转回金融服务贸易。</p><p>■ Share 股，股份:〔某人应得或应负担的〕一份:</p><p> the &#39;lion&#39;s share (of sth)  最大(或最好)的一份</p><p>The firm has captured the lion&#39;s share of the UK market.这家公司已经占有了英国最大的市场份额。</p><p>share consolidation股份合并</p><p>share of market市场占有率；市场份额</p><p>share premium股票溢价</p><p>■ten·ure /  /noun U</p><p>1. the right to stay permanently in a teaching job〔大学教师的〕终身职位，终身教席，终身教职:</p><p>•It&#39;s becoming increasingly difficult to acquire academic tenure .要获得终身教职现在越来越难了。</p><p>2. Formal the period of time when someone has an important job〔重要职位的〕任期:</p><p>•The company has doubled in value during his tenure.在他的任期内，公司的市值翻了一番。</p><p>3. Law the legal right to live in a house or use a piece of land for a period of time〔房屋的〕居住权;〔土地的〕使用期</p><p>—tenured adj:</p><p>•a tenured position终身职位</p>",

            "title": "初中英语写作（二）", 
            "content": "<p>以下是Hersey根据大型考试的批卷经验总结的评分标准，在此只列出可供学生们参考的前两档中的总体原则，下面当然还分有很多评分细则，不予说明：</p><p>1. 优秀 （19---16分）</p><p>写出全部要点；语言优美且准确无误，行文连贯，表达清楚，文中使用一些高级词汇、从句、关联词语等。（在此基础上，如果能写出真情实感，事例新颖典型，字迹工整且没有任何语法错误，可以得满分。）</p><p>2. 好 （15---11分）</p><p>缺少要点，语言基本准确，行文基本连贯，表达基本清楚。</p><p>大家可以看出，要点全是优秀作文的第一标准（具体的框架写法请翻上一篇文章“中考专项之英语写作（一）”），孩子们只要英语基础还不错，能写出有内容的句子就很好达成。那么怎样使你的文章达到优秀中的上线标准呢？我们要从语言的使用上下功夫，比如，能用复合句的地方不用简单句，能用短语的地方不用单词，能引用名言的情况不用自己的语言。以下是写作中的常见表达，大家尽可能地背下来，在日常写作中应用，那么你的写作技能就会不知不觉地提高了。</p><p>呈现观点的句式：</p><p>In my opinion,</p><p>Ithink/believe that</p><p>From my point of view,</p><p>As far as I am concerned,</p><p>事例开头句式：</p><p>I still remember when I was …years old,</p><p>Let me share a story with you.</p><p>I will never forget …</p><p>总结性句式：</p><p>Above all,</p><p>In a word,</p><p>To sum up,</p><p>In conclusion,</p><p>All in all,</p><p>其他常用句式：</p><p>It is adj. to do sth.</p><p>so… that …</p><p>(not) as…as</p><p>(这个太多了，不能一一列举了，就是平时积累的句式尽量多用，不要只写简单的主谓宾，主系表结构。)</p><p>高级词汇：</p><p>表转折对比关系：although; however</p><p>表因果：because; as a result (of);</p><p>表事件发生顺序：first; second; after that; finally;</p><p>表并列补充关系：what’s more; besides; in addition; as well as; not only…but (also);</p><p>谚语名言：</p><p>Where there is a will, there is a way.</p><p>有志者事竟成</p><p>Action speaks louder than words.</p><p>行动胜过语言</p><p>Well begun, half done. </p><p>好的开始等于成功的一半</p><p>A journey of a thousand miles begins with a single step. 千里之行，始于足下</p><p>full of beans 精力旺盛</p><p>jump out of my skin 吓我一跳</p><p>……</p><p>最后，敲黑板！中考阅卷方式为网上阅卷，因此，一定要有适中的篇幅（词汇量要够，但是不能超出上限太多）和美观的卷面（干净工整）！</p><p>写作是最能体现一个人的知识积累和综合运用语言的能力，需要长期、有目的地去坚持练习，才会有质的飞跃，孩子们加油吧！</p>",

            "title": "初中英语写作（一）", 
            "content": "<p>作为一名初中一线英语教师，深知孩子们在英语写作上的苦恼。大多数的学生对英语作文是相当地排斥，见到题目就是三个字——“不会写”，甚至是一些英语功底一流的学生，每次考试作文也只能拿到13、14分（满分20）。其实，英语写作是有诀窍的，只要英语基础不是太差，掌握了方法，16分以上是没问题的。接下来，Hersey就针对沈阳地区中考英语写作题型进行说明。</p><p>首先，无论是语文写作还是英语写作，只要是考试，第一步也是最重要的当然是“审题”，英语写作的审题尤其重要，因为题干就是评分标准。沈阳市近几年来写作题型基本都是一致的，以2018年中考题为例。题干是这样的：</p><p>B）英国作家萨克雷曾说：“播种习惯收获性格，播种性格收获命运。”在生活中，一定有好的习惯伴随你的成长。请你以Good habits make me ________为题写篇短文（词数80到100）。步骤与要点如下：</p><p>1.确定主题，并在文中说明原因；</p><p>2.围绕主题，进行叙述；</p><p>3.写出具体计划，也可以讲述一段与主题有关的故事或经历。</p><p>要求：</p><p>1. 补全标题（参考词汇：better, happier,healthier, stronger等）；</p><p>2. 字迹工整，内容完整连贯，语言准确规范；</p><p>3. 鼓励写出真情实感，对紧扣主题的适当发挥不予扣分。短文的开头已给出，不计入总词数；</p><p>4. 作文中可以写出具体计划内容，也可以使用亲身经历或虚构的故事，但要注意时态的运用；如果参照短文中的内容，不可以直接引用短文中的句子；</p><p>5. 作文中不要出现考生和相关人物的真实校名和姓名。</p><p>Good habits make me________</p><p>Good habits are important in our lives.They influence us a lot in many ways. I think …</p><p>以上题干，Hersey给大家简单总结为三要素：标题；原因；事例【计划、故事、经历三选其一】。当然，三要素一定要一致，原因要指向观点，事例要指向原因+观点。</p><p>接下来，怎样开始写呢？我们通常要以三部分来完成写作。</p><p>第一部分，观点+原因。如I think good habits make me healthier.（观点） With good habits, I can live a regular life.（原因）</p><p>第二部分，也是最重要的部分——事例。本部分是作文的主体部分，事例一定要突出中心，支持自己的观点成立。首先，三选一，计划要用将来时态进行叙述，故事、经历要用过去时态。个人认为经历最好写，也最有说服力。最简单的写法就是Time-Place-Character-Beginning-Middle-Ending，也就是大家熟悉的记叙文六要素了。如：I can still remember the experience of the summer holiday before Ibecame a junior high school student, I had a large amount of free time. I choseto play computer games all day and all night to relax. Sometimes I even forgotto have dinner. At last, I got very sick and went to hospital. The doctor toldme that I must keep good habits such as eating on time and doing exercisesregularly. From then on, I changed my lifestyle. I woke up early and wentjogging every morning; I had every meal regularly, and so on. As a result, Ibecame healthier and healthier.</p><p>第三部分，总结。目的是升华主题，发出畅想、号召等。如：In my opinion, keeping good habits is the most helpful way to keephealthy. If you want to become healthier, it is high time that you should keepgood habits.</p><p>批卷老师一般会直接找到上面的三要素，要点全，语言还可以，就属于一档作文啦。下一期的中考英语写作，Hersey会大概说明各档作文的评分标准，以及在要素全的基础上怎样得超高分哦，请持续关注。</p><p>另：虽然Hersey以沈阳地区考题为例讲解，但全国的义务教育课程标准是统一的哦。</p><p>附《英语课程标准》（2011年版）中语言技能分级标准中对于“写”的要求:1.能根据写作要求，收集、准备素材。2、能独立起草短文、短信等，并在教师的指导下进行修改。3、能使用常见的连接词表示顺序和逻辑关系。4、能简单描述人物或事件。5、能根据图示或表格写出简单的段落或操作说明。</p>",

            "content": "<p>经济学人双语精读五期招新，邀请你上车啦，请到公众号了解课程。</p><p>  思维导图</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b7c292ef7220a9ec601af8b6f30ac6b2_b.jpg\"
