width=&#39;450&#39; height=&#39;338&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"450\" data-rawheight=\"338\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"450\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7c29623bc3d3b1d23d03bc00cb305a1c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7c29623bc3d3b1d23d03bc00cb305a1c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-6d73576dfe26887ba8f4660568da0d8b_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"213\" data-rawheight=\"180\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"213\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;213&#39; height=&#39;180&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"213\" data-rawheight=\"180\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"213\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-6d73576dfe26887ba8f4660568da0d8b_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>台北-蒙马特影像咖啡馆</b></p><p>属于深宵的巴黎印象</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4d4903168a8b9156bf6caab290b903ba_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"450\" data-rawheight=\"337\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"450\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4d4903168a8b9156bf6caab290b903ba_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;450&#39; height=&#39;337&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"450\" data-rawheight=\"337\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"450\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4d4903168a8b9156bf6caab290b903ba_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4d4903168a8b9156bf6caab290b903ba_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>台北咖啡馆，或者是台北人对饮食的文化，未曾体验过，也一定听闻过。基本上，台北人习惯城市咖啡文化，几乎可以说生活在咖啡世界。台北最火的咖啡热话已转到一系列的山区咖啡馆。蒙马特影像咖啡馆，馆主赖岳忠本是一位台北著名的人像摄影师。因他喜爱巴黎，很想在台北寻回巴黎的气味，所以在阳明山一角辟出属于自己的咖啡新天地，想要释放一点巴黎的咖啡香气。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0d5d5470f381dbb3f0ccd4fab1449982_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"935\" data-rawheight=\"600\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"935\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0d5d5470f381dbb3f0ccd4fab1449982_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;935&#39; height=&#39;600&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"935\" data-rawheight=\"600\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"935\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0d5d5470f381dbb3f0ccd4fab1449982_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0d5d5470f381dbb3f0ccd4fab1449982_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>有识之士在台北开设咖啡馆值得庆幸，因不乏捧场客趁夜幕低垂之际从老远城中前来落脚，咖啡馆最繁忙之时正是由晚饭后开始。馆子分三个区域，分别是馆前的露天茶座、主馆和后馆。炎夏的台北，户外茶座也大有人坐，可见年轻一辈对咖啡文化钟爱有加。主馆及后馆内布局有如古老朴素的美术馆，馆内也腾出偌大的空间来放置一张床，俨然一副下午茶的格局。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><u>地址：台北市士林区菁山路131巷13号</u></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e7da6c20d922de7b541acc41c400aa34_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"450\" data-rawheight=\"337\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"450\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e7da6c20d922de7b541acc41c400aa34_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;450&#39; height=&#39;337&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"450\" data-rawheight=\"337\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"450\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e7da6c20d922de7b541acc41c400aa34_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e7da6c20d922de7b541acc41c400aa34_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-d87181ae905c6a0062644c220472d4eb_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"213\" data-rawheight=\"180\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"213\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;213&#39; height=&#39;180&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"213\" data-rawheight=\"180\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"213\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-d87181ae905c6a0062644c220472d4eb_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>巴厘岛-Alila Manggis</b></p><p>返璞归真</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4af64114d3e0acdc51938ca7aa953ca8_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4af64114d3e0acdc51938ca7aa953ca8_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;640&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4af64114d3e0acdc51938ca7aa953ca8_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4af64114d3e0acdc51938ca7aa953ca8_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>诚然，这里的咖啡味道不能算是很美味的那一种，但别具创意的Food Concept，加上十分家庭式的茶座感觉，令人自在逍遥！爱上这家小咖啡餐馆，爱它的全面性，菜单是包罗万象，具时尚感觉之余，食物又有现代人所谓的Contemporary口味。当然，更重要的一点是便宜的价钱却又有高级的服务。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-685cfe3711d5e0a0fb9303ba999459a7_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"480\" data-rawheight=\"321\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"480\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-685cfe3711d5e0a0fb9303ba999459a7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;480&#39; height=&#39;321&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"480\" data-rawheight=\"321\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"480\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-685cfe3711d5e0a0fb9303ba999459a7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-685cfe3711d5e0a0fb9303ba999459a7_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>开业近2年的To Die For，装潢上仍居潮流最前沿。这里闻名的甜食，配上了咖啡别具一种风味。吃To Die For的甜食配咖啡，应该是一种感觉，一种童年快乐无拘无束的自由感觉。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><u>地址：Desa Buitan, Manggis, Karangasem Regency, Bali</u></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-e92c0f51b556228ae470b61abf56048e_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"400\" data-rawheight=\"600\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"400\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;400&#39; height=&#39;600&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"400\" data-rawheight=\"600\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"400\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-e92c0f51b556228ae470b61abf56048e_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-531835bb975198ae3afc010135319ff6_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"213\" data-rawheight=\"180\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"213\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;213&#39; height=&#39;180&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"213\" data-rawheight=\"180\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"213\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-531835bb975198ae3afc010135319ff6_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>安特卫普-Het Pomphuis</b></p><p>巨型泵房</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-8c0902de390a402634110f8721ed9ef5_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"576\" data-rawheight=\"374\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"576\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-8c0902de390a402634110f8721ed9ef5_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;576&#39; height=&#39;374&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"576\" data-rawheight=\"374\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"576\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-8c0902de390a402634110f8721ed9ef5_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-8c0902de390a402634110f8721ed9ef5_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>Het Pomphuis坐落于安特卫普海港旁一座旧建筑，是一座由造船泵房改建成的咖啡馆、餐厅与酒吧混合体。咖啡馆名叫Het Pomphuis，荷兰语意指The Pump House，建于1918年的泵房，是当时欧洲最大型的铁铸泵房。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-fba38ed0f9bd6386a3e2b5f1ff574408_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"333\" data-rawheight=\"500\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"333\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;333&#39; height=&#39;500&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"333\" data-rawheight=\"500\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"333\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-fba38ed0f9bd6386a3e2b5f1ff574408_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-3c6c4640d69ac757cbb7af508cb69d0c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"506\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-3c6c4640d69ac757cbb7af508cb69d0c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;750&#39; height=&#39;506&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"506\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-3c6c4640d69ac757cbb7af508cb69d0c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-3c6c4640d69ac757cbb7af508cb69d0c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>Het Pomphuis咖啡馆只占整座泵房的前三分一范围，中央部分的木地板被挖空，泵房全景一目了然。餐厅范围由泵房楼层特设的餐桌VIP专位开始，延伸至最深处的广阔用餐区。天花板换成玻璃透入日光，环绕室内如钢铁般的冷感稍得缓和。咖啡厅座位围绕水泵房7米之上，距天花板达13米高。俯瞰三座已镇守差不多一百年的铁铸水泵，鲜见宝绿色墙色与挂在墙上的铁铸电话，即使水泵再没有迸发出隆隆巨响，广阔空间仿佛凝重地描绘建筑背后的故事，徐徐坠入往日的场景故事里。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><u>地址：Siberiastraat, Antwerp 2030, Belgium</u></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-8c87be0d8fb229ab5653ea7c528eb339_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"650\" data-rawheight=\"431\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"650\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-8c87be0d8fb229ab5653ea7c528eb339_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;650&#39; height=&#39;431&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"650\" data-rawheight=\"431\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"650\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-8c87be0d8fb229ab5653ea7c528eb339_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-8c87be0d8fb229ab5653ea7c528eb339_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-a36c41fb70c82482ee2ea79ded0b11a4_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"1000\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-a36c41fb70c82482ee2ea79ded0b11a4_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;750&#39; height=&#39;1000&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"1000\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-a36c41fb70c82482ee2ea79ded0b11a4_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-a36c41fb70c82482ee2ea79ded0b11a4_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-4397f70f8cf12bc2eb7341c7c4e55bc5_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"213\" data-rawheight=\"180\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"213\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;213&#39; height=&#39;180&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"213\" data-rawheight=\"180\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"213\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-4397f70f8cf12bc2eb7341c7c4e55bc5_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>斯德哥尔摩-无名咖啡馆</b></p><p>暂时忘记一切</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>姓名、身份不再重要了；为了咖啡馆，辞掉了工作，全心全意投入短暂美味的咖啡世界！也许，只有斯德哥尔摩人，才会对“自家理想”爱得如此疯狂。这一所无名咖啡馆位于斯德哥尔摩现代美术馆（Moderna Museet）外的小船坞上，只在夏季开放。咖啡馆本该就是修船工人出没的热点，店主偏偏要在这里开设咖啡小店。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-331720879795c938e86ce135c479c2f3_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"450\" data-rawheight=\"308\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"450\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-331720879795c938e86ce135c479c2f3_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;450&#39; height=&#39;308&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"450\" data-rawheight=\"308\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"450\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-331720879795c938e86ce135c479c2f3_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-331720879795c938e86ce135c479c2f3_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>从外形看来，小店是艘引路入港口的拉船。进门处有长长木条（破落但颇具艺术感），客人像走平衡线般进入店东的海洋咖啡茶座。无名咖啡馆，只有餐台四张，在烟囱两旁，既是咖啡茶座也是客人互诉心声的地方。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>大概找遍整个斯德哥尔摩市，没有比这里更有自然理想的同时又开阔人们生活视野的“咖啡馆”了吧。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><u>地址：在Moderna Museet外的小船坞上碰碰运气吧</u></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-595b91c5f459d5834bf8c8a863f4f9c1_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"751\" data-rawheight=\"88\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"751\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-595b91c5f459d5834bf8c8a863f4f9c1_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;751&#39; height=&#39;88&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"751\" data-rawheight=\"88\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"751\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-595b91c5f459d5834bf8c8a863f4f9c1_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-595b91c5f459d5834bf8c8a863f4f9c1_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>推荐</p><p>享受一杯好喝的咖啡</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2cc60c36b863de0519f5d84e17f19070_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1002\" data-rawheight=\"668\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1002\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2cc60c36b863de0519f5d84e17f19070_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1002&#39; height=&#39;668&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1002\" data-rawheight=\"668\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1002\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2cc60c36b863de0519f5d84e17f19070_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2cc60c36b863de0519f5d84e17f19070_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>凡仕小磨王，革命性设计</p><p>小身材，大磨力，你值得拥有</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>策划、出品 | 凡仕咖啡</p><p>监制 | Olivia</p><p>图片 | 部分来自网络<br/></p><p>编辑 | Yvonne</p><p>设计 | 高涵</p><hr/><p>更多精彩，请关 注【凡仕咖啡的世界】。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>原创文章，版权归作者所有。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>未经著作权人同意，不得直接使用及转载。</p><p></p><p></p><p></p><p></p>",

            "title": "【英语语法】一般现在时还能表示过去和将来？", 
            "content": "<p>咱们在一般现在时（<a href=\"https://zhuanlan.zhihu.com/p/42340055\" class=\"internal\">私房英语小灶：【英语语法】动词篇——一般现在时</a>）这一讲里面说过除了标配用法，它的特殊用法有：</p><ul><li>运动解说、演示说明、动作描述、剧情介绍、（剧本中）舞台动作说明、指引道路、图片说明</li></ul><p><b>总结起来就是——说明</b></p><p>用现在时来表达有种现场感，就酱。</p><p>咱们这一篇来说一下一般现在时更特殊的用法。</p><h2><b>一、表示将来</b></h2><p><b>表示按规定、时间表、计划或安排要发生的事情，有一个表示未来的时间状语</b></p><p>这一点咱们之前也说了，举几个例子：</p><ul><li>The plane takes off at 11:30 and arrives in Shanghai at 1:20.</li><li>The show begins at seven and ends at ten.</li><li>Is there a film on tonight?   </li></ul><p><b>时间或条件从句中，表将来</b></p><p><b>（关于时间从句、条件从句，请参看</b><a href=\"https://zhuanlan.zhihu.com/p/39824547\" class=\"internal\">【英语语法】从句篇——状语从句①（图文讲解）</a>，<a href=\"https://zhuanlan.zhihu.com/p/39912472\" class=\"internal\">【英语语法】从句篇——状语从句②（图文讲解）</a><b>）</b></p><ul><li>I&#39;ll give her the telex when she comes.</li><li>Turn off the lights before you leave.</li><li>If we hurry, we may catch the bus.</li></ul><p><b>其他从句中，谓语以一般现在表示将来（这个不常见，考纲之外）</b></p><ul><li>I hope it keeps fine for a few more days.</li><li>Suppose he doesn&#39;t agree, what shall we do?</li><li>He will continue the work no matter what happens.  </li></ul><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c10262ead4ff5b3cd649bb31598d99ce_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"594\" data-rawheight=\"69\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"594\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c10262ead4ff5b3cd649bb31598d99ce_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;594&#39; height=&#39;69&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"594\" data-rawheight=\"69\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"594\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c10262ead4ff5b3cd649bb31598d99ce_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c10262ead4ff5b3cd649bb31598d99ce_b.jpg\"/></figure><h2><b>二、表示过去</b></h2><p><b>少数情况下可以表示过去，只限于少量动词，如hear, say, tell等（这个也不常见，考纲之外）</b></p><ul><li>I hear you are moving.</li><li>Diana says you told her to come over here.</li><li>Oh, I forget where she lives. </li></ul><p>这些动作发生的时间在说话人脑中已经模糊不重要，他主要说明从句所表示的情况。</p><p><b>此外还有：故事中的描绘、标题与章节标题、引用（这个知道就行，不用纠结）</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><i>参考书目：</i></p><p><i>《张道真英语语法（全新版）》</i></p>",

            "url": "https://zhuanlan.zhihu.com/p/43025479", 
            "userName": "英语主播皮卡丘", 
            "userLink": "https://www.zhihu.com/people/8956a4cdf96cd8f39f1d0205687037f0", 
            "upvote": 5, 
            "title": "“月光族”用英语怎么说？钱包空空如也！", 
            "content": "<p>英文中有很多表达字面上说的是一回事，而实际意思却完全是另外一回事。如果我们仅依照字面意思去理解，肯定会闹出不少笑话。为了避免这种尴尬的情况，我们就需要做好积累的工作。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>1. Paycheck to Paycheck</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e9d8919e60d6c876164a48685f3b3530_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"240\" data-rawheight=\"240\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e9d8919e60d6c876164a48685f3b3530_b.jpg\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"240\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;240&#39; height=&#39;240&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"240\" data-rawheight=\"240\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e9d8919e60d6c876164a48685f3b3530_b.jpg\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"240\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e9d8919e60d6c876164a48685f3b3530_b.gif\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>Paycheck 表示薪水支票。过着从一张到薪水支票到下一张薪水支票的生活就说明你的生活没有什么结余。也就是我们所说的“月光族”。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>例句：</b></p><p>A great number of people find themselves living paycheck to paycheck.</p><p>大多数人都感觉自己是“月光族”。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>2. face the music</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-62f2987407593e78572634e1b05e0774_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"427\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-62f2987407593e78572634e1b05e0774_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-62f2987407593e78572634e1b05e0774_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;427&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"427\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-62f2987407593e78572634e1b05e0774_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-62f2987407593e78572634e1b05e0774_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-62f2987407593e78572634e1b05e0774_b.gif\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>这个俚语的字面意思是“面对音乐”。在以前歌剧表演时，演员都是面对着坐在乐池中为他们伴奏的乐师们的。如果他们站在台上忘词了，那他们就只能尴尬的站在舞台上面对着乐师了。慢慢的，这个俚语演化出了勇敢面对后果，承担惩罚的含义。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>例句：</b></p><p>You have made your choice. Now you&#39;ll have to face the music.</p><p>既然你已做出抉择，你就得勇敢地承担一切后果。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>3. Working around the clock.</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-79f7bcac0ae5d8d34b2ead535e48ce9d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"456\" data-rawheight=\"262\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"456\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-79f7bcac0ae5d8d34b2ead535e48ce9d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;456&#39; height=&#39;262&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"456\" data-rawheight=\"262\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"456\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-79f7bcac0ae5d8d34b2ead535e48ce9d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-79f7bcac0ae5d8d34b2ead535e48ce9d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>Around the clock在这里表达的是整整一天的24个小时。当你在表周围绕一圈工作时就表明你已经非常的忙碌了。</p><p>英文释义：When you&#39;re working around the clock, you&#39;re busy all day and all night long. Around the clock means for an entire 24-hour day.</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>4. She&#39;s working on my last nerve.</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-02c2430a2365048b3444d6def99f3850_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"281\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-02c2430a2365048b3444d6def99f3850_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-02c2430a2365048b3444d6def99f3850_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;500&#39; height=&#39;281&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"281\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-02c2430a2365048b3444d6def99f3850_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-02c2430a2365048b3444d6def99f3850_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-02c2430a2365048b3444d6def99f3850_b.gif\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>Nerve代表的是神经。My last nerve 是指自己的最后一条神经。之前的神经都已经被你折磨断了，最后一条再断了我就要爆发了！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>例句：</b></p><p>Please, shut up! You&#39;re working on my last nerve.</p><p>请闭嘴，你在挑动我的最后一根神经！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>5. Greek gift</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>希腊人的礼物（×）</p><p>害人的礼物（√）</p><p>该词组源自《木马屠城记》：在特洛伊战争中，希腊人将藏满士兵的木马送进特洛伊城，灭亡了特洛伊灭亡。“Greek gift”指“图谋害人的礼物”。推荐大家可以看看布拉德·皮特主演的电影Troy（《特洛伊》）。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>例句：</b></p><p>Ware his gift, that is a Greek gift!</p><p>小心他的礼物，那是包藏杀机的礼物！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>这些俚语，你都了解了吗？</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>切记：</b></p><p>如果你想加入有外国人、<b>大学生的微信群（英语角）练口语，关注微信公众号“竖起耳朵听”即可加入</b>，那里会美音、伦敦腔、印度腔的小伙伴都有。</p>",

            "upvote": 15, 
            "title": "回答“Thank you”最全的10种方式，你会吗", 
            "content": "<p><b>1.My pleasure./It&#39;s my pleasure.乐意效劳；这是我的荣幸。</b><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>这一句回答相当客气并且有礼貌，可以用来回答那些你乐于热心帮助的人，也可以显示你的热情。这句话比“You&#39;re welcome”更加正式，语气也强。通常男生们会在女生面前显示一下自己足够绅士，用上这句话。你还可以说，“It was my pleasure.”或者“Pleasure is all mine.”</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>2.Sure/Sure thing.应该的</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>你相信吗？这是美国人最常见的回答方式之一，但是飞儿打赌90%的人都没学过，并且不知道能这么说。你肯定会疑惑，用Sure回答不是“当然”的意思吗？几乎每个去美国的中国人，都会对老美回答“sure”感到愕然——我说一句“谢谢”，你说一句“是的，当然”，这哪里是感谢的态度？</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>其实我们误会美国人了，这个“当然”指的是“帮助别人是理所当然的”，并不是“说谢谢是理所当然的”。现在你可以理解sure的语境了：没什么，我帮助你是应该的。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-0b3bc424025eb56e5c5a5ef24090c7eb_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"510\" data-rawheight=\"300\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"510\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-0b3bc424025eb56e5c5a5ef24090c7eb_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;510&#39; height=&#39;300&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"510\" data-rawheight=\"300\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"510\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-0b3bc424025eb56e5c5a5ef24090c7eb_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-0b3bc424025eb56e5c5a5ef24090c7eb_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>3.Of course!没事，这是当然的</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>这个词和sure相似，都是对于“帮助是理所当然的”说法的省略。不过，对于非美国人用这句话也有可能会引起误会，这个要注意。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>4.You bet!当然的；不客气；不用谢</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>很美式口语的说法，在美国比较多人使，若非地道美国人,或是在美国待过一阵子,很少人会知道You bet.</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>5.Anytime.别客气，随时愿为您效劳。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>Anytime 这个词的本意是“任何时候，无论何时”。当别人说“谢谢”的时候，你说 anytime就表示“别客气，(无论何时都)愿为您效劳”的意思。口语里，还可以说anytime my friend，对陌生人甚至也可以这样讲，很礼貌。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b6bca019c63ec2b796ee3b64605c90ac_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"335\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b6bca019c63ec2b796ee3b64605c90ac_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;500&#39; height=&#39;335&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"335\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b6bca019c63ec2b796ee3b64605c90ac_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b6bca019c63ec2b796ee3b64605c90ac_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>6.Happy to help!很开心能帮到你！</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>这是一种很普通但是比较不俗套的说法，意思也很清晰，当别人道谢的时候，你说“帮到你我很开心”，很自然的回应。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>7.You got it.你明白的，心照</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>想想，“你抓到精髓了”,意思就是“你对了,你明白了”在美剧里经常会看到当别人说Thank you的时候用”You got it“来回答,通常是好友、好兄弟之间最常见。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>8.No worries.没问题。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>在澳大利亚可能会更常用一些，意思就是不用担心啦(do not worry about that), 也可以说 “that&#39;s alright”, 或者 “sure thing”。这句话，给人感觉很友好风趣，有一种澳洲的兄弟情义。在美语里，也可以说 “no problem”或者 “not a problem”。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2997a656cd4d374c182801276c6b8d08_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"338\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2997a656cd4d374c182801276c6b8d08_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;500&#39; height=&#39;338&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"338\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2997a656cd4d374c182801276c6b8d08_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2997a656cd4d374c182801276c6b8d08_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>9.No sweat. 小意思！</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>“Sweat”在英文里是“汗水”的意思，no sweat，你可以理解为一滴汗也没出就把事情办好了。是不是听上去很够意思呢？</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>10.That&#39;s all right.不用谢；不客气；没关系。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>right这个词有“正确、恰当”的意思。That’s all right的字面意思就是“一切都没什么不妥”，演变成“没关系”的意思。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>切记：</b></p><p>如果你想加入有外国人<b>、大学生的微信群（英语角）练口语，关注微信公众号“竖起耳朵听”即可加入</b>，那里会美音、伦敦腔、印度腔的小伙伴都有。</p>",

            "title": "Are we good到底什么意思？很多学生都不懂", 
            "content": "<p>上课时，外教巴拉巴拉说了一堆，你一直没说话，外教突然问你：“Are we good？”是不是顿时手足无措？说就说吧，咋还问&#34;我们好不好&#34;，这和讨论有半毛钱关系吗？皮卡丘告诉你，外教才不是问&#34;我们好不好&#34;，而是在说……</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>1、Are we good到底是什么意思?</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>场景一：</b></p><p>在和别人讨论问题的时候，如果对方问你Are we good? 不是问你&#34;我们好吗&#34;？(我们好不好还用问~)，而是在问你听懂了吗?</p><p>Are we good?=你理解了吗？(你和我是一个频道的不~~)</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-17acdb744046d5cb75d1143a5368ec95_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"360\" data-rawheight=\"210\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-17acdb744046d5cb75d1143a5368ec95_b.jpg\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"360\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;360&#39; height=&#39;210&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"360\" data-rawheight=\"210\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-17acdb744046d5cb75d1143a5368ec95_b.jpg\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"360\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-17acdb744046d5cb75d1143a5368ec95_b.gif\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>例句:</b></p><p>- Are we good?</p><p>你明白(我的意思)吗?</p><p>- Yeah, absolutely!</p><p>是的，当然理解!</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>场景二</b></p><p>如果你和别人闹不愉快，他对你说Are we good? 是在问你&#34;我们和好了吗？&#34;(还生气不?)</p><p>Are we good=我们和好了吧?(表生气了嘛~~)</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-323e4289b43dfbaa90e00db9516a1349_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"498\" data-rawheight=\"273\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-323e4289b43dfbaa90e00db9516a1349_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"498\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-323e4289b43dfbaa90e00db9516a1349_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;498&#39; height=&#39;273&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"498\" data-rawheight=\"273\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-323e4289b43dfbaa90e00db9516a1349_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"498\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-323e4289b43dfbaa90e00db9516a1349_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-323e4289b43dfbaa90e00db9516a1349_b.gif\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>例句:</b></p><p>Are we good? Are you still angry with me?</p><p>我们和好了吗?你还生我的气吗?</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>2、Good sense是&#34;好感&#34;?</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>看到good sense，就翻译成&#34;好感&#34;的宝宝，小编只能无奈地说：你真的是在直译的路上，走得越来越远了啊!</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>Good sense＝判断力强(最强大脑)</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f5dfff65c7f1c41366451b137c245619_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"406\" data-rawheight=\"195\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f5dfff65c7f1c41366451b137c245619_b.jpg\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"406\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;406&#39; height=&#39;195&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"406\" data-rawheight=\"195\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f5dfff65c7f1c41366451b137c245619_b.jpg\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"406\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f5dfff65c7f1c41366451b137c245619_b.gif\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>例句:</b></p><p>She showed a lot of good sense.</p><p>她表现出惊人的判断力.</p><p>那“好感”应该怎么说?</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>正确表达:</b></p><p>Good opinion=好感(只是觉得人不错~)</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ff6cefd22cbf9a3d07c11a70e4c499d6_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"303\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ff6cefd22cbf9a3d07c11a70e4c499d6_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ff6cefd22cbf9a3d07c11a70e4c499d6_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;500&#39; height=&#39;303&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"303\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ff6cefd22cbf9a3d07c11a70e4c499d6_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"500\" class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>例句:</b></p><p>I have a good opinion to him.</p><p>我觉得他人还不错.</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>更高级的表达:</b></p><p>favorable impression=好感.好印象(可用于表白)</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>例句:</b></p><p>Although he left a favorable impression on me, I still refused to date him.</p><p>虽然他表示对我有好感，我还是拒绝了。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>3、Good time是&#34;好时间&#34;?（</b>当然不是啦！）</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>场景一</b></p><p>如果人家说 Is this a good time to talk to you? 就是在说：这个时间和你谈话合适吗? good在这里表示&#34;合适的，方便的&#34;。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>good time=合适的时间=方便的时间</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>例句:</b></p><p>When would be a good time to phone?</p><p>什么时间打电话合适呢？</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>场景二</b></p><p>如果你出去玩耍，别人对你说：Have a good time! 就是在祝你玩得愉快啦!</p><p>good在这里表示&#34;愉快的&#34;Good time=愉快的时光<br/></p><p             "url": "https://zhuanlan.zhihu.com/p/41313728", 
            "userName": "Richard Li", 
            "userLink": "https://www.zhihu.com/people/39090a91904511b1bb5c36321eeb1117", 
            "upvote": 4, 
            "title": "粗谈笛卡尔在第一哲学沉思录中犯的错误", 
            "content": "<p>                            Some Flaws Descartes Made in <i>Meditations on First Philosophy</i></p><p>     In the 17th century, because of the invention of telescope, a lot of unsetting discoveries were made. For example, before the invention of telescope, people believed that Jupiter was a lonely celestial body. However, with the telescope, people started to know that there were actually four moons surrounding it. Changes like this could easily make an individual to doubt what he used to believe in. Influenced by these discoveries, Descartes started to think that whether he was right about<br/>everything he used to believe in.  </p><p>     In the Meditation One, Descartes questions the most fundamental way we use to<br/>perceive the world, which is through our senses. Using the cases of hallucination and insanity, he assumes that we can be deceived by our senses; as a result, our senses are not trustworthy. In addition, he makes an assumption that the omnipotent God could be deceiving us all the time about everything so that there is nothing we can trust (59-63). In Meditation Two, Descartes states that even though there is the always possibility that God could be deceiving us, there is one thing he cannot change which is the fact that he was thinking. In other words, he is &#34;a thinking thing&#34;. On the second half of the Meditation Two, Descartes used the phase changes of wax to prove that even though the shape and property of wax can change from solid to liquid and back to solid, it is still the wax any way. He wants to use this to prove that the existence of actual objects. In Meditation Three, Four and Five, Descartes proved that the God exists, and he won&#39;t deceive us. In Meditation Six, Descartes illustrate that we are actually perceiving the world through our souls which is also the difference distinguish human from animals and material objects (Descartes, 31-33). </p><p>     Some of the arguments in the Meditations of First Philosophy seems reasonable but there are still three few points that are worthy of our deep reflection.  </p><p>     First and foremost, after doubting the certainty of “a man” and “a body”, Descartes concluded that he was “a thinking thing”. However, the certainty of “thing” still can be doubted since it’s not clear or distinct what that is when one says: “I am a thing”. The only thing Descartes proved in the first two Meditations is that no one can deceive him about the fact that he was thinking. As a result, the only clear and<br/>distinct idea here is the thought. In the bundle theory, &#34;the mind itself, far from being an independent power, is simply &#39;a bundle of perceptions&#39; without unity or cohesive quality” (Maurer); and, in this light, the mind is not “a thing”. In addition, it’s not correct to say that I am “&#39;a bundle of perceptions” because the only medium people exist on is the thought in one&#39;s mind. However, you can never have the exact same thought again just like the fact that &#34;everything changes, and nothing remains still ... and ... you cannot step twice into the same stream&#34; (Seneca). Therefore, you are never the thought that existed before. Moreover, as you know you were thinking, the<br/>thought has already faded away, so the statement that “I am a thought” is still not certain enough. Nevertheless, no one can doubt that the thought has existed which means that “I” somehow existed. In conclusion, I can say that “I was a thought”. The reason I use “was” is because it avoids the objection stated above, and it gives “I” and “thought” the property of existing in the past.</p><p>     The second problem is in <i>Meditations</i> Three, Four and Five. In the latter part of the first <i>Meditation</i>, he assumed that the entity which could be deceiving him is an evil genius. However, in the <i>Meditation</i> Three, Four and Five, he abandons the phrase “evil genius” and starts to use “God” again. Moreover, his way of proving he is not deceived by an omnipotent thing is based on the understanding of the Christian God, which is “infinite, independent, supremely intelligent and supremely powerful, and that created me along with everything else that exist-if anything else exists” (Descartes, 76), and later he explains that the God is perfect and even morally. However, among all these properties the only necessary one (according to Descartes’s own proof) God’s being is “infinite”. </p><p>     First of all, God does not have to be independent in order to deceive us, since beyond that God there can still be other Gods that are manipulating our god. This can be more understandable if we take the movie <i>Matrix</i> as an example. In the movie, Neo took the red pill and entered the actual world. This process is like a tree-dimensional creature that suddenly has the property of a four-dimensional object. However, what about the possibility that the “actual world” is still a programmed “dream”? This shows what the Gods beyond our God would be like. </p><p>     Secondly, the reason our senses can be wrong is that neither of our senses can understand any three-dimensional objects perfectly. For example, the image from our eye is two-dimensional, which means that we cannot know how it looks from the top, back or bottom. We can call this a dimensionality reducing perception, which means that even without anything deceiving us, we just cannot understand anything perfectly correct. In the same time, we can understand any two-dimensional objects thoroughly so that I am making a hypothesis that any four-dimensional creatures can understand the three-dimensional objects perfectly and cannot be deceived on this. </p><p>     In addition, to us, it&#39;s undeniable that 2+3=5. However, to an infinite object, it is not exactly the case. Let give “a” the identity of “2+3” and give “b” the identity of “any real number”. Since (lim x-&gt;infinity) a/x=0 and, (lim x-&gt;infinity) b/x=0. As a result, to infinity, “a” is actually identical to “b”. To God, who is proven to be infinite, will not even consider deceiving us about the problem of two plus three since to him, our perception of numbers is meaningless. In addition, this can be used on most knowledge we have. </p><p>     Nevertheless, there is an interesting hypothesis stated in the book <i>The Three Body Problem </i>and it is called the Rancher Theory suggesting there is still a way that we can<br/>be deceived. Assume that there is a rancher that feeds his turkey every noon at 11 o’clock. On the Thanksgiving Day, the scientist turkey gathered everyone and announces that he has a huge scientific breakthrough which is there will be food every 11 0’clock. After that, every turkey starts to wait. When the hand of the clock turns to 11, the rancher rushes to the farm and sends them all to the dining tables. </p><p>     In general, <i>Meditation </i>Three, Four and Five doesn’t really prove that God exist since without God we still can’t get things perfectly correct. Even if the God exist, there is no way to prove that he is morally perfect and won’t deceive us. </p><p>     Finally, in <i>Meditation </i>Six, Descartes claims that we won&#39;t be deceived if we are  using rational thinking, and it’s apart from our body which is like a non-separate soul. In <i>Discourses on Method</i>, Descartes discusses more about the soul and claims that it’s the major difference between human and animals plus materials. However, what will rational thinking be if it can be materialized？</p><p>     In the field of physics, there is a famous scientific hypothesis called Laplace&#39;s demon:</p><p>“We may regard the present state of the universe as the effect of its past and the cause of its future. An intellect which at a certain moment would know all forces that set nature in motion, and all positions of all items of which nature is composed, if this intellect were also vast enough to submit these data to analysis, it would embrace in a single formula the movements of the greatest bodies of the universe and those of the<br/>tiniest atom; for such an intellect nothing would be uncertain and the future just like the past would be present before its eyes.” (Pierre Simon Laplace).</p><p>Clearly, it assumes that our thoughts can be represented as the forces in the nature. In this way, there is no need to doubt everything’s existence since the existence of thoughts is the effect or the respond to actual object or event which can also be understood as forces. In this way, doubting the existence of things around us is like a gear in a big machine doubting the whole network. </p><p> In conclusion, there are three very doubtful assumptions in the <i>Meditations on First Philosophy</i>, which are proven by the uncertainty of “thing”, the uncertainty of God’s properties and existence, and the uncertainty of free will&#39;s existence. As said, we can use the phrase “I was a thought” to replace the phrase “I am a thinking thing” (Descartes, 65). We have to admit that if God doesn’t exist, we can never get<br/>things perfectly right and if God exist, there is no way to prove that he won&#39;t deceive us, as in the case of the rancher. Theoretically, our rational thinking can be understood as an event responding to the forces surrounding us and it&#39;s unnecessary to doubt the existence of objects around us. </p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>Work Cited</p><p>Descartes, Rene. Discourses on Method and Meditations on First Philosophy. 4th ed., Hackett Publishing Company Indianapolis. 1998, pp.60. </p><p>Liu, Cixin. The Three Body Problem. National Aeronautics and Space Administration; for sale by the Office of Technical Services, Dept. of Commerce. 1964. </p><p>Maurer, The Reverend Armand. &#34;Western philosophy. Basic Science of Human Nature in Hume&#34;. Encyclopædia Britannica. 2013.</p><p>Seneca, “L. ANNAEI SENECAE EPISTULARUM MORALIUM AD LUCILIUM LIBER SEXTUS”, <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.thelatinlibrary.com/sen/seneca.ep6.shtml\" class=\" external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\"><span class=\"invisible\">http://www.</span><span class=\"visible\">thelatinlibrary.com/sen</span><span class=\"invisible\">/seneca.ep6.shtml</span><span class=\"ellipsis\"></span></a></p>",

            "content": "<p>之前皮卡丘读到了一句话：Then President Trump buttered up President Xi by playing a video of his granddaughter singing songs in Mandarin.（“butter up拍马屁，奉承”）其实“拍马屁”在英语里有不少说法，文明程度也不一样，今天就教大家一些“拍马屁”的英文表达。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c1d23b3b80e799311d7b79a402a0bd6e_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"301\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c1d23b3b80e799311d7b79a402a0bd6e_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;500&#39; height=&#39;301&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"301\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c1d23b3b80e799311d7b79a402a0bd6e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c1d23b3b80e799311d7b79a402a0bd6e_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>1.Stop flattering me like that. <br/>别再那样拍我马屁。</p><p><br/>2. I don&#39;t like Peter. He&#39;s such a brown-noser. 我不喜欢彼得。他真是个马屁精。</p><p><br/>3. I know he&#39;s trying to butter me up, but I&#39;m not buying it.<br/>我知道他想要拍我马屁，但我才不吃那一套。 <br/><br/>4. In order to get the promotion, she kept apple-polishing the manager.<br/>为了升迁，她一直在拍经理的马屁。</p><p><br/>5. He started sucking up to the boss as soon as he got on board.<br/>他一来公司就开始拍老板的马屁。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a035208d33bfadcad887cf26440e2c45_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"419\" data-rawheight=\"300\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"419\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;419&#39; height=&#39;300&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"419\" data-rawheight=\"300\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"419\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a035208d33bfadcad887cf26440e2c45_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>6. The professor likes her because she knows how to please him.<br/>教授喜欢她是因为她知道怎么讨好他。 <br/><br/>7. She&#39;s very good at paying lip service.<br/>她很会讲一些言不由衷的好听话。</p><p><br/>8. Everyone in this company knows that he&#39;s trying to curry favor with the board of the directors.<br/>公司里的每一个人都知道他想要巴结董事会。</p><p><br/>9. That guy is a real bootlicker.<br/>那个家伙真是个马屁精。 <br/><br/>10. You want me to kiss his ass? Read my lips: No Way! <br/>你要我拍他马屁？仔细听好：门儿都没有！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>切记：</b></p><p>如果你想加入有外国人、<b>大学生的微信群（英语角）练口语，关注微信公众号“竖起耳朵听”即可加入</b>，那里会美音、伦敦腔、印度腔的小伙伴都有。</p>",

            "content": "<p>学习英语的同时，多关注一下外国人常说的口语，这样交流起来才会更加方便。在日常对话里，外国人，尤其是美国的年轻人喜欢用口头禅，在非正式场合可以使交流更自然。今天皮卡丘就教大家说说外国人经常使用的一些口头禅。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>01 Look 你听我说</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2256db05855ce0a8b1c379fc96cf58c5_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"268\" data-rawheight=\"268\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2256db05855ce0a8b1c379fc96cf58c5_b.jpg\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"268\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;268&#39; height=&#39;268&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"268\" data-rawheight=\"268\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2256db05855ce0a8b1c379fc96cf58c5_b.jpg\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"268\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2256db05855ce0a8b1c379fc96cf58c5_b.gif\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>Look, I&#39;m really sorry I woke you, I just wanted to tell you I was all right.</p><p>听我说，我真抱歉吵醒你，我只是想告诉你我一切都好。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>02 Like I said 就像我刚才说的</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-dd2df9c119b168076c03a7af45d061fd_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"220\" data-rawheight=\"220\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-dd2df9c119b168076c03a7af45d061fd_b.jpg\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"220\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;220&#39; height=&#39;220&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"220\" data-rawheight=\"220\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-dd2df9c119b168076c03a7af45d061fd_b.jpg\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"220\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-dd2df9c119b168076c03a7af45d061fd_b.gif\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>Like I said before, I see failure as a stepping stone to success.</p><p>就像我之前说的，失败是成功之母。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>03 Well 回应对方之前可以说的</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-896369acefb6c105b57a0f6280dd4fd7_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"280\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-896369acefb6c105b57a0f6280dd4fd7_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-896369acefb6c105b57a0f6280dd4fd7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;500&#39; height=&#39;280&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"280\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-896369acefb6c105b57a0f6280dd4fd7_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-896369acefb6c105b57a0f6280dd4fd7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-896369acefb6c105b57a0f6280dd4fd7_b.gif\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>- Where did you go last month?</p><p>你上个月去哪呢?</p><p>- Well, I was in America.</p><p>这个嘛，我在美国呢。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>04 You know 希望得到对方的理解</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-d1f522c069c8ecd7cf7ca928d5f09637_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"350\" data-rawheight=\"196\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-d1f522c069c8ecd7cf7ca928d5f09637_b.jpg\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"350\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;500&#39; height=&#39;243&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"243\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-e8c469c611a10e9dfef6d7e963a28d7f_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-e8c469c611a10e9dfef6d7e963a28d7f_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-e8c469c611a10e9dfef6d7e963a28d7f_b.gif\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>I know you&#39;ve been studying chimpanzees for thirty years now.</p><p>我知道你研究黑猩猩至今已有30年了。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>07 Here&#39;s the thing 问题是</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d92bfe552e76315e4cd025bf748f54d5_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"212\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d92bfe552e76315e4cd025bf748f54d5_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d92bfe552e76315e4cd025bf748f54d5_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;500&#39; height=&#39;212&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"212\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d92bfe552e76315e4cd025bf748f54d5_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d92bfe552e76315e4cd025bf748f54d5_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d92bfe552e76315e4cd025bf748f54d5_b.gif\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>Here&#39;s the thing, we don&#39;t have that much money for the trip.</p><p>问题是，我们没有那么多钱去旅行。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>08 You know what I&#39;m saying? 你懂我的意思吗?</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-3dd6db520739dfddb199c9a5021b0410_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"320\" data-rawheight=\"180\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-3dd6db520739dfddb199c9a5021b0410_b.jpg\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"320\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;             "upvote": 2, 
            "title": "“You're cute”不能乱说，容易得罪人！", 
            "content": "<p><b>1、You&#39;re cute不能乱说！</b></p><p>cute最基本的意思是可爱，但更多时候被用来描述小动物，小宝宝。如果对成年人说You&#39;re cute，外国人会想，难道你把我当小动物或小孩子，幼稚鬼了吗！非常容易造成误会。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>例句：</b></p><p>①Your puppy is so cute.</p><p>你养的小狗真可爱。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>②What a cute baby. Look at how big his eyes are.</p><p>这个小宝宝真可爱，看看他的眼睛有多大。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>表达&#34;可爱&#34;这样说：</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>“Lovely”本身是可以翻译成“可爱的;令人愉快的;亲切友好的;慷慨大方的”；同时，做名词时意思为“美女，美人，漂亮的佳人”。所以尤其当男生用“Lovely”来赞美女生，女孩子可是会很开心的哦~</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>例句：</b></p><p>She is a lovely girl.</p><p>他是一个很可爱的女孩子。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-630d585e7610fb2216384c36ba445dd3_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"270\" data-rawheight=\"270\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-630d585e7610fb2216384c36ba445dd3_b.jpg\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"270\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;270&#39; height=&#39;270&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"270\" data-rawheight=\"270\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-630d585e7610fb2216384c36ba445dd3_b.jpg\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"270\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-630d585e7610fb2216384c36ba445dd3_b.gif\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>2、外国人怎么使用cute？</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>同性之间说cute，它意思可以是&#34;萝莉，正太，鲜肉&#34;，女生机灵，聪慧，娇小，惹人爱，男生超级帅，很好看。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>例句：</b></p><p>①I met a cute guy in the park.</p><p>我刚才在公园遇到一个超级帅的男生。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>②There is one girl in 101 group that&#39;s super cute.</p><p>在创造101里，有个小姐姐特别可爱。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>异性之间说cute，这里就和可爱没关系了，尤其在美式口语，cute的意思就变成委婉的说sexy，包含强烈感情色彩，觉得对方性感，漂亮，吸引人。你对异性说You&#39;re so cute，外国人会误认为你对他有好感。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>例句：</b></p><p>①I met this cute guy at a party and we&#39;re going out next week.</p><p>我在聚会上遇到一个帅哥，下周我们要出去约会了哦。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>②There was this girl, she was really cute.</p><p>就那个女孩，她非常性感。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>3、cute还能表示&#34;平淡无奇&#34;</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>我们聊这个女生，长的一般，放在人堆里也找不到的那种，不知道用什么词，一般会说，她很可爱，其实就是她很普通，英文对应的词，就是cute，当你真的喜欢一个女生，你一定会说，oh, I like her a lot!或 she is something她与众不同。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>- How do you like her?</p><p>你觉得她怎么样？</p><p>- Oh, she&#39;s cute.</p><p>她挺可爱的（呵呵哒）。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-450c9ac88e5c4d96c1918eeee498a9a6_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"270\" data-rawheight=\"270\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-450c9ac88e5c4d96c1918eeee498a9a6_b.jpg\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"270\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;270&#39; height=&#39;270&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"270\" data-rawheight=\"270\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-450c9ac88e5c4d96c1918eeee498a9a6_b.jpg\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"270\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-450c9ac88e5c4d96c1918eeee498a9a6_b.gif\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>4、act cute难道是表演可爱？</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>师傅，我坚持不住啦！这种可爱的行为，在英文里就叫act cute，act是表演，行动，那么act cute，就是表演可爱，也就是我们常说的&#34;卖萌&#34;啦~</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>例句：</b></p><p>He knows how to act cute to get her heart.</p><p>他知道怎么卖萌来赢得她的心。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ae43f041fdc799c574c37e76c5bc21bf_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"400\" data-rawheight=\"400\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"400\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;400&#39; height=&#39;400&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"400\" data-rawheight=\"400\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"400\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ae43f041fdc799c574c37e76c5bc21bf_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>5、cute in it是说你&#34;里面很可爱吗？&#34;</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>在想什么呢，直译的同学，要打屁屁啦，in是指穿的衣服，in red其实就是穿红色衣服，cute有漂亮性感的意思，所以是在说，你穿这件衣服真好看。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>例句：</b></p><p>Dear, you really look cute in that dress.</p><p>亲呐，你穿这条裙子真好看呀。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>总结：想夸奖别人可爱，一定要注意cute的使用环境，不然可就闹误会啦！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>切记：</b></p><p>如果你想加入有外国人、大学生的微信群（英语角）练口语，关注微信公众号“竖起耳朵听”即可加入，那里会美音、伦敦腔、印度腔的小伙伴都有。</p>",

width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;532&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"532\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6f48aa8f8f64334085d1dca58b67afbe_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6f48aa8f8f64334085d1dca58b67afbe_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6007bb2a1c6d94ec18777f8aa3166036_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"532\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6007bb2a1c6d94ec18777f8aa3166036_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;532&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"532\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6007bb2a1c6d94ec18777f8aa3166036_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6007bb2a1c6d94ec18777f8aa3166036_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>宿务地区<b>最早引入斯巴达式</b>教学管理模式的学校</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>▲ 每天8课时的正规授课、加上自习、俱乐部活动等，每天约有11课时的密集安排；</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5567f5408c4a7fcf9fd43973db7af67b_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"532\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5567f5408c4a7fcf9fd43973db7af67b_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;532&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"532\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-da1eda1e6730ac9ba8fc8ec9230b8dfb_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-da1eda1e6730ac9ba8fc8ec9230b8dfb_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>▲ 提供半斯巴达和斯巴达<b>两种模式</b>共学生选择，也可以中途更换模式。（斯巴达是严格学习时间管理，平日不能外出，只能在校园内学习或休息，周五下午下课后及周末才能外出.半斯巴达通常可以外出，但是有一定条件限制，如当日考试需满足分数要求才能外出。）</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>▲ 宿务设施条件最好的英语学校之一。新校区整体占地面积5200平方米。设计风格简洁大气，室内宽敞明亮。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-00d05eb0708edd13af3efa56908d7d1c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"532\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-00d05eb0708edd13af3efa56908d7d1c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;532&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"532\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-00d05eb0708edd13af3efa56908d7d1c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-00d05eb0708edd13af3efa56908d7d1c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d9ba2bf69b52fe72b141895730c21b80_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"532\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d9ba2bf69b52fe72b141895730c21b80_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;532&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"532\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d9ba2bf69b52fe72b141895730c21b80_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d9ba2bf69b52fe72b141895730c21b80_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>▲ 24小时安保管理，及50个摄像头监控。建校以来从未有安全事故发生。</p><p>▲ 教师水平保障。EV的全体讲师参加ITAA (International TESOL Accreditation Authority) 主办的TESOL课程并顺利结业；校方每月安排讲师培训，以保证在职讲师不断提升自身教学技能。</p><p>▲ TOEIC、IELTS、TOEFL考试课程、商务英语课程、都是从老校区延续下来的，有着非常丰富的教学经验。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>课程内容</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-541d64ecedd63b4ff68da141e15cc355_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"792\" data-rawheight=\"595\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"792\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-541d64ecedd63b4ff68da141e15cc355_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;792&#39; height=&#39;595&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"792\" data-rawheight=\"595\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"792\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-541d64ecedd63b4ff68da141e15cc355_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-541d64ecedd63b4ff68da141e15cc355_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>▲每节课5分钟的休息时间。大多数学校是50分钟的哦。目前应该是菲律宾课时最长的了。通常上起课来很紧凑，课间就只够上个厕所和找教室了。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-5b6346a85f5c1165adcfdeec197032a6_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1089\" data-rawheight=\"725\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1089\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-5b6346a85f5c1165adcfdeec197032a6_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1089&#39; height=&#39;725&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1089\" data-rawheight=\"725\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1089\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-5b6346a85f5c1165adcfdeec197032a6_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-5b6346a85f5c1165adcfdeec197032a6_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>雅思保分（5.5/6.0/6.5）</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>&gt; IELTS 5.5 保分班入学条件：IELTS 官方测试成绩4.0或同等英 语水平</p><p>&gt; IELTS 6.0 保分班入学条件：IELTS 官方测试成绩5.0或同等英语水平</p><p>&gt; IELTS 6.5 保分班入学条件： IELTS 官方测试成绩6.0</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>▲每节课5分钟的休息时间。大多数学校是50分钟的哦。目前应该是菲律宾课时最长的了。通常上起课来很紧凑，课间就只够上个厕所和找教室了。</p><p>-----------------</p><p>● 一对一（4课时）<br/> ● 小组（2课时 ）</p><p>● 大团体（2课时）: grammar for IELTS, Practice Test<br/> ● 单词测试: 早点名，7:00之后15分钟左右完成。<br/> ● 句子测试: 晚上19:00之后，约需要15分钟，记忆约50个句子。<br/> ● 强制自习：19:00~22:00 。</p><p>------------------<br/></p><p>▲保证班要求10周参加雅思官方考试（费用自行承担），如果没有获取目标分数，可免学费继续学习，但是住宿费、签证延期等当地费用需要学员自己承担。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d02d1044c7f260fc18181682423111a9_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"134\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d02d1044c7f260fc18181682423111a9_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; Idiom、Vocabulary &amp; Grammar practice、Writing;</p><p>● 团体课（2课时）：Grammar、Presentation、Listening、Active &amp; Speak up四选二。 监护人也可以选择一般成人课程。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>青少年课程（青少年游学团）</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a7f208795bc586b27d906db469fbe1c1_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"469\" data-rawheight=\"666\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"469\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a7f208795bc586b27d906db469fbe1c1_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;
