            "upvote": 0, 
            "title": "原来“top banana顶级香蕉”这么厉害，以前真是低估！", 
            "content": "<p>看到“top banana”，小伙伴是不是想到了放在最高处的香蕉，又或者是想到了质量最优，“高处不胜寒”的香蕉？</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-de8b3a4726614702b503646aeeaa1452_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"203\" data-rawheight=\"204\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"203\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;203&#39; height=&#39;204&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"203\" data-rawheight=\"204\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"203\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-de8b3a4726614702b503646aeeaa1452_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>那么top banana在英语口语里到底是什么意思呢？</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>1）正确含义：第一把手，即“大老板、领导人、掌权者”。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>2）来源：</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>原来早在100年前美国还没有电影、电视的时候，有一种舞台演出，内容包括流行音乐、舞蹈和笑话。有时人们会在一个讲笑话的演员说完一个笑话之后给他一个香蕉。渐渐地人们就把最滑稽的演员称为top banana。</p><p>如今人们还会把“电视上演闹剧的人”叫做top banana，但更多时候你能够在提到政坛、经济圈中重要人物、第一把手的时候看到这个词组。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>3）例句：</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>For many years Doctor Henry Kissinger has been a top banana in American foreign policy. He is no longer in public office but plenty of people still listen to his advice.</p><p>许多年来，亨里·基辛格博士在美国外交政策方面是最高级的一位官员。现在他已经不再担任公职，但是许多人仍然愿意听取他的意见。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>He is a top banana in this corporation.</p><p>他是公司的老板。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f1fbcc897e50b34f6b8c9e29066b0b8d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"276\" data-rawheight=\"133\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"276\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;276&#39; height=&#39;133&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"276\" data-rawheight=\"133\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"276\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f1fbcc897e50b34f6b8c9e29066b0b8d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>还有一些短语用来描述重要的人物，或者至少自以为重要的人：</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>1. top brass 高级军官；要员</b></p><p>top brass和 top banana有其相似之处，但是对象不同。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>1）来源：</b></p><p>top banana这个说法比较随便，而top brass这个说法原先来自军队，比top banana更加尊重一些。brass就是黄铜。但是，top brass里的 brass是来自美国军帽帽舌上那金颜色的编织物。刚开始的时候，top brass是指军队里的高级将领。但是，在战争结束后，top brass也应用于商业界的重要人物。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>2）例句：</b>See that guy selecting potato chips over there? Don&#39;t mistake him as an ordinary person like you and me. He&#39;s the top brass in our company, with the power to hire or fire anybody in the whole outfit.</p><p>看见那边在挑土豆片的那个人吗？你别以为他是像你我一样的普通人。他可是我们公司里的重要人物，有权在整个公司里雇用人，也有权解雇职工。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-df8cd6c54f99ee9b746c4c3ad19c1bde_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"300\" data-rawheight=\"228\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"300\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;300&#39; height=&#39;228&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"300\" data-rawheight=\"228\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"300\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-df8cd6c54f99ee9b746c4c3ad19c1bde_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>2. big wheel 具有影响力的人</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>1）来源：</b></p><p>big wheel在第二次世界大战后成为流行用语。这个短语可能来自安装卡车或小汽车组件的人多年来使用的短语。他们说，如果一个人比较重要，比较有影响力，那么由他来转动大轮（一般大轮带着小轮转）。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>2）例句：</b></p><p>Harry was the big wheel in his class.</p><p>哈利是他们班上的大人物。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c12df1a09ebc94296bf59737120f7f28_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"225\" data-rawheight=\"225\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"225\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;225&#39; height=&#39;225&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"225\" data-rawheight=\"225\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"225\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c12df1a09ebc94296bf59737120f7f28_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>今天的表达你学会了吗？</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>切记：</b></p><p>如果你想加入有外国<b>人、大学生的微信群（英语角）练口语，关注微信公众号“竖起耳朵听”即可加入</b>，那里会美音、伦敦腔、印度腔的小伙伴都有。</p>",

            "title": "中国人最容易说错的8句英语，你用过吗？", 
            "content": "<p><b>1. 我非常喜欢它。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>I very like it .✘</p><p>I like it very much.</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>2. 这个价格对我挺合适的。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>The price is very suitable for me. ✘</p><p>The price is right.</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>suitable(合适的、相配的)最常见的用法是以否定的形式出现在告示或通知上。</p><p>如：</p><p>The program is not suitable for children.</p><p>这个节目儿童不宜。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-0abf18d6babcff22bf600a9ba28ad379_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"335\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-0abf18d6babcff22bf600a9ba28ad379_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;500&#39; height=&#39;335&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"335\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>3. 你是做什么工作的呢？</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>What’s your job? ✘</p><p>What do you do?</p><p>what’s your job?这种说法难道也有毛病吗？是的。因为如果您的谈话对象刚刚失业，如此直接的问法会让对</p><p>方有失面子，所以建议问：<br/></p><p>Are you working at the moment?</p><p>目前您是在上班吗？</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>接下来您才问：</b></p><p>Where are you working these days?</p><p>目前您在哪儿工作呢？</p><p>What line of work are you in?</p><p>或者您从事哪个行业呢？</p><p>顺带说一下，回答这类问题时不妨说得具体一点，不要只是说经理或者秘书。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>4. 用英语怎么说？</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>How to say? ✘</p><p>How do you say this in English?</p><p>How to say?是在中国最为泛滥成灾的中国式英语之一，这决不是地道的英语说法.</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>同样的句子有：</p><p>How do you spell that please?</p><p>请问这个词如何拼写？</p><p>How do you pronounce this word?</p><p>请问这个单词怎么读？</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>5. 明天我有事情要做。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>I have something to do tomorrow. ✘</p><p>Sorry but I am tied up all day tomorrow.</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>用I have something to do.来表示您很忙，这也完全是中国式的说法。因为每时每刻我们都有事情要做，躺在那里睡大觉也是事情。所以您可以说我很忙.I’m tied up.(脱不开身)</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>还有其他的说法：</p><p>I can’t make it at that time.</p><p>I’d love to, but I can’t.</p><p>I have to stay at home.</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>6. 我想我不行。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>I think I can’t. ✘</p><p>I don’t think I can.</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>这一组然是个习惯问题，在语法上称为否定前置，这就是汉语里面说“我想我不会”的时候，英语里面总是说“我不认为我会”。以后您在说类似的英语句子的时候，只要您留心，也会习惯英语的说法的.</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5ef79e4a2ccf7d8a6f25aeb1af82c157_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" 我的舞也跳得不好。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>I don’t dance well too. ✘</p><p>I&#39;m not a very good dancer either.</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>当我们说不擅长做什么事情的时候，英语里面通常用not good at something，英语的思维甚至直接踊跃到：我不是一个好的舞者。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>8. 现在几点钟了？</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>What time is it now? ✘</p><p>What time is it?</p><p>What time is it now?这是一个直接从汉语翻译过的句子，讲英语的时候没有必要说now,因为您不可能问what time was it yesterday? 或者what time is it tommorow?</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>还有一种说法是：</p><p>How are we doing for time?</p><p>这句话在有时间限制的时候特别合适.</p><p <br/>This describes everything you are not.</p><p>善良、聪慧、多情而性感， <br/>可惜这些你一条都不占。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5b459f8f9a2f23b9560dd1b15deb57ab_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"281\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5b459f8f9a2f23b9560dd1b15deb57ab_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;             "content": "<p><b><i>我使用一个译者。抱歉，如果我的中国人是坏的，我不是一名当地中国演讲人!</i></b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>在这篇文章上，我们将谈论用于美国经常的共同的英语成语。因为它将帮助您听起来更多象一个说母语的人，学会成语是非常重要的。</p><p>这些经常也用于电影和电视节目，因此学会这些是重要的!</p><p><b>您是否是准备好？我们去!</b></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-27f98a3cb047305b98973c1b663ba878_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"2730\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-27f98a3cb047305b98973c1b663ba878_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;4096&#39; height=&#39;2730&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"2730\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-27f98a3cb047305b98973c1b663ba878_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-27f98a3cb047305b98973c1b663ba878_b.jpg\"/></figure><ol><li><b>A blessing in disguise</b></li></ol><p><b>定义:</b> 最初是坏的,但是现在是好</p><p><b>例子: </b>Failing his exams was <b>a blessing in disguise</b>, for he realized that he was not enjoying his class and decided to try a different class.</p><p>2. <b>A dime a dozen</b></p><p><b>定义:</b> 共同的事</p><p><b>例子: </b>Those chairs are very beautiful, but they are <b>a dime a dozen</b>, I have seen them at every store.</p><p>3. <b>Beat around the bush</b></p><p><b>定义: </b>避免通常说什么您意味,因为它是难受的</p><p><b>例子: </b>If you want to ask me, just ask, don&#39;t <b>beat around the bush!</b></p><p>4. <b>Better late than never</b></p><p><b>定义: </b>迟是好与不到达比较</p><p><b>例子: </b>It&#39;s okay if you are late to the meeting, <b>better late than never.</b></p><p>5. <b>Bite the bullet</b></p><p><b>定义: </b>结束某事,因为是不可避免的</p><p><b>例子: </b>The lazy man decided to <b>bite the bullet </b>and start exercising, so he joined a local gym.</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b><i>了不起的工作!您几乎完成!</i></b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"small\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-630769fd495013749ef1d578f53feb40_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"small\" data-rawwidth=\"1508\" data-rawheight=\"2262\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1508\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-630769fd495013749ef1d578f53feb40_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1508&#39; height=&#39;2262&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"small\" data-rawwidth=\"1508\" data-rawheight=\"2262\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1508\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-630769fd495013749ef1d578f53feb40_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-630769fd495013749ef1d578f53feb40_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>6. <b>Break a leg</b></p><p><b>定义: </b>好运</p><p><b>例子: </b>Have fun during your performance, <b>break a leg!</b></p><p>7. <b>Call it a day</b></p><p><b>定义: </b>停止工作在某事</p><p><b>例子: </b>Let&#39;s <b>call it a day, </b>I am very tired and need to go home.</p><p>8. <b>Cut me some slack</b></p><p><b>定义: </b>给某人在他们的品行的某一余地</p><p><b>例子:</b> Sorry I could not attend the party, I had so much homework,<b> cut me some slack.</b></p><p>9. <b>Cutting corners</b></p><p><b>定义: </b>不足做某事为了存时间或金钱</p><p><b>例子: </b>The government<b> cut corners </b>when they built the school with bad materials, and put everyone in danger.</p><p>10. <b>Easy does it</b></p><p><b>定义: </b>减速</p><p><b>例子: </b>Don&#39;t drive so fast,<b> easy does it!</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>做的井!我希望您享受这篇文章。留下下面评论!</b></p>",

Which one?</p><p>中国银行？哪一家？</p><p>B：The one near Chaoyang Park.</p><p>朝阳公园旁边的那个。</p><p>A：That&#39;s OK. Please fasten the seat belt.</p><p>好的。请系好安全带。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-22cf5b9383920ff6b82f9b391e9d3076_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"513\" data-rawheight=\"300\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"513\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-22cf5b9383920ff6b82f9b391e9d3076_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;513&#39; height=&#39;300&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"513\" data-rawheight=\"300\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"513\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-22cf5b9383920ff6b82f9b391e9d3076_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-22cf5b9383920ff6b82f9b391e9d3076_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>2.请给我发票 Please Give Me the Inovice　</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>A：Here is the fare. Please give me the inovice.</p><p>这是车费。请给我发票。</p><p>B：Here you are.</p><p>给你。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>3.请在拐角处停车 Please Stop at the Corner</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>A：Now we are at the station.</p><p>我们到火车站了。</p><p>B：Please stop at the corner.</p><p>请在拐角处停车。</p><p>A：That&#39;s all right.</p><p>好的。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-97942d129324dd08115cdea80cf8cbbb_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"294\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-97942d129324dd08115cdea80cf8cbbb_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;500&#39; height=&#39;294&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"294\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-97942d129324dd08115cdea80cf8cbbb_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-97942d129324dd08115cdea80cf8cbbb_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>4.现在不是上下班高峰期 It Is Not the Rush Hour</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>A：We&#39;ll get there within 20 minutes.</p><p>我们会在20分钟内到的。</p><p>B：I&#39;m afraid there will be a traffic jam.</p><p>恐怕会遇到塞车。</p><p>A：Don&#39;t worry. We have to hurry up.</p><p>好的。我们要快一点。</p><p>A：Do you think I can make it?</p><p>你认为我能按时到吗？</p><p>B：No problem. We can arrive there in half an hour.</p><p>没问题。我们会在半小时内到达。</p><p>A：Half an hour? But it&#39;s 2:30 now!</p><p>半小时？但是现在已经两点半了！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>6.请不要吸烟好吗？ Would You Please Stop Smoking?</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>7.别开得太快 Please Don&#39;t Drive Too Fast</b></p><p><b>----分割线------</b></p><p><b>切记：如果你想加入有外国人、大学生的英语社群，关注我的公众号“竖起耳朵听”英语角里</b>会伦敦腔、美音、印度腔的小伙伴都有！找到它就能一起交流。</p>",

            "title": "【英语学习随笔】2善用英语中的小词", 
            "content": "<p>中午吃饭的时候像往常一样刷一条的视频，今天的采访对象是一位低调的英国奶奶，她的曾曾祖父是大名鼎鼎的达尔文，她本人是英国炙手可热艺术家。具体采访的细节大家可以翻看今天一条的推送，这个视频对我感触比较深的是老奶奶的英语表达，非常朴实和准确，对于我们平时学习出国留学考试的同学有很好的学习价值。我举视频结尾的四句话为例。</p><blockquote>Being famous is not important to me. I think success is a very personal achievement. You could be having difficulties with your family. Or you could have great success in how you have managed that. That is being successful. </blockquote><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><blockquote>Being famous is not important to me.</blockquote><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6110c9a783b9c7ef85364ee4ee0fa256_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2001\" data-rawheight=\"1125\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"2001\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6110c9a783b9c7ef85364ee4ee0fa256_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;2001&#39; height=&#39;1125&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2001\" data-rawheight=\"1125\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"2001\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6110c9a783b9c7ef85364ee4ee0fa256_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6110c9a783b9c7ef85364ee4ee0fa256_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>第一句话非常简短，主系表，sth be important to sb的结构大家也都熟悉，但是平时在教学当中我发现同学大多数时候不会第一时间想到being famous的表达而是绞尽脑汁想famous的名词形式，即把这个句子写成Fame is not important to me. 但fame这个词本身比being famous更正式和书面一些，相比而言没有being famous的亲和力强，字幕也非常应景地将being famous翻译成了“出名”，如果用fame的话估计会翻译成“名声”或者“声誉”了。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><blockquote>I think success is a very personal achievement. </blockquote><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-416cc13c68d90cbddf1fe37418687549_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2001\" data-rawheight=\"1125\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"2001\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-416cc13c68d90cbddf1fe37418687549_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;2001&#39; height=&#39;1125&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2001\" data-rawheight=\"1125\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"2001\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-416cc13c68d90cbddf1fe37418687549_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-416cc13c68d90cbddf1fe37418687549_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>第二句话有两个小词我们可以学会使用：personal，achievement。当我们想说每个人对于某件事情持不同的态度的时候，不要随便用different将就一下，可以学会使用personal，比如说 it is a personal choice/decision。除此之外，大多数同学可能会习惯地使用thing来指代所有的事物，英国老奶奶使用的词是achievement，与平淡无味的thing相比，achievement更能突出过程中付出的努力和最后结果达成的成就感。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><blockquote>You could be having difficulties with your family. </blockquote><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b4fc0d9b6e1b6453d9c45c77a0a2d9a0_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2001\" data-rawheight=\"1125\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"2001\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b4fc0d9b6e1b6453d9c45c77a0a2d9a0_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;2001&#39; height=&#39;1125&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2001\" data-rawheight=\"1125\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"2001\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b4fc0d9b6e1b6453d9c45c77a0a2d9a0_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b4fc0d9b6e1b6453d9c45c77a0a2d9a0_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>第三句话我们可以学习其中的be+doing的形式表示动作正在进行的状态，老奶奶想表达是家庭生活当中我们会无时无刻碰到许多困难，如果直译的话大家可能会说constantly have many difficulties，虽然非常直白但是少了这份对生活的理解和含蓄的美，既然学会了进行时我们就要在正确的场合多去使用它。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><blockquote>Or you could have great success in how you have managed that. </blockquote><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-41aeeda3d740f755ea94ce55ff831f75_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2001\" data-rawheight=\"1125\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"2001\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-41aeeda3d740f755ea94ce55ff831f75_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;2001&#39; height=&#39;1125&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2001\" data-rawheight=\"1125\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"2001\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-41aeeda3d740f755ea94ce55ff831f75_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-41aeeda3d740f755ea94ce55ff831f75_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>第四句话老奶奶举出她对成功的理解即成功地维系好一个家庭，manage这个词本身即可表示成功做好某事，避免了使用successfully finish／accomplish带来的浮夸感和重复感。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><blockquote>That is being successful. </blockquote><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-162f35932c22f693cee4a4cfb46aff3b_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2001\" data-rawheight=\"1125\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"2001\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-162f35932c22f693cee4a4cfb46aff3b_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;2001&#39; height=&#39;1125&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2001\" data-rawheight=\"1125\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"2001\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-162f35932c22f693cee4a4cfb46aff3b_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-162f35932c22f693cee4a4cfb46aff3b_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>大家可能觉得为啥要把英语学得这么细致，我们生活中都会有这样的经验，有些人一张嘴我们就知道TA的社会背景，我们也希望自己在国外不会张口就是beautiful，huge，very的川普式英语。哦，对了，我查了一下老奶奶的背景信息，她是大学教授。</p><hr/><p></p>",

            "content": "<p><b>我使用中国译者。我抱歉，如果我的中国人是坏的，我不来自中国。</b></p><p>我知道很多中国人民要改进他们的英语。在这篇文章上和在其他未来文章上，我将提供您以技巧关于怎样提高您的英语技能。</p><p>学会一种新的语言总是一个难题!但是，与坚苦工作和坚持不懈，您能完成任何东西!</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-b408c0ded5df02b77ff1df0af694e4b7_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1280\" data-rawheight=\"605\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1280\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-b408c0ded5df02b77ff1df0af694e4b7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1280&#39; height=&#39;605&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1280\" data-rawheight=\"605\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1280\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-b408c0ded5df02b77ff1df0af694e4b7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-b408c0ded5df02b77ff1df0af694e4b7_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>确信，并且不要害怕犯错误。如果您需要帮助，不要是害羞的讲话，您总是能消息我。</p><p>设法围拢自己与英语。下载在您的电话的英语学习应用并且听英语歌曲。如果您能，尝试总是在英语环境里。</p><p>建立一个惯例并且设法至少一天一次学习。越多您学习，越容易将变得习性。很快，因为它将变得自动，您不会必须考虑学习。</p><p>告诉许多人民，您能关于您的研究计划。如果您忘记，让他们提醒您学习!并且，如果他们不是分心，您能邀请他们学习与您。两个人比一个总是好!</p><p><b>读书，文字，讲话和听</b>是您将需要学会的核心技能。这些技能要求成为大师在英语。很快，因为您将是优秀的在它，您教您的朋友和家庭英语。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-1a224f29a6e641614547f59d75edf6dc_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1280\" data-rawheight=\"880\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1280\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-1a224f29a6e641614547f59d75edf6dc_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1280&#39; height=&#39;880&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1280\" data-rawheight=\"880\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1280\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-1a224f29a6e641614547f59d75edf6dc_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-1a224f29a6e641614547f59d75edf6dc_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>您在英语笔记本不知道也不了解的记录新的词。使用新的词在句子并且背诵他们每天，直到您了解他们。</p><p>确定天的最佳的时候学习为您。每个人是不同的。我喜欢在晚上学习，但是我认识喜欢早晨学习的某些人。您决定!</p><p>词是更加容易记住您是否能记住句子词得用于。例如，如果您不可能记住词“<b>bark</b>”，然后一个句子例如”A dog likes to<b><i>bark</i></b>“也许是有用的。</p><p>告诉我您是否喜欢这篇文章。我将继续张贴更多文章类似于此。谢谢读并且如下写下评论。</p><p><b>I hope you are having a blessed and wonderful day! =)</b></p>",

            "title": "“Have two left feet”不是有“两只左脚”", 
            "content": "<p>如果想要学好英语，和歪果仁一样地道，除了标准的发音外，你还得要懂俚语，这样才能和歪果仁无障碍交流。今天给大家分享几个关于数学的俚语，看看真正的意思你都知道吗？</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-faa95e983c8a4580533c2d88681770cf_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"334\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-faa95e983c8a4580533c2d88681770cf_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;500&#39; height=&#39;334&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"334\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-faa95e983c8a4580533c2d88681770cf_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-faa95e983c8a4580533c2d88681770cf_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>1、five-and-ten</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>它的本意不是“五和十”而是指“廉价商品；杂货店，小零售店”</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>例句：</b></p><p>The meat is five- and -ten recently.</p><p>最近肉很便宜。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>怎么理解five-and-ten表示廉价商品意思？原来five-and-ten是five-and-ten-cent store的简写，美国人说习惯了就直接说five-and-ten，这里的five表示5分钱，ten表示1角钱。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>还有美国人说成five-and-dime 这里的dime[ daim ] (美、加拿大)一角银币。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>例句：</b></p><p>In a five-and-ten-cent store you can buy all manner of things.</p><p>在小杂货店里你能买到各种各样的东西。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>2、Deep six</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>它不是“深六”正确意思是“丢掉，置之不理”</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>例句：</b></p><p>The agency gave my suggestions the deep six.</p><p>经销处对我的建议置之不理。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>We have to give all our plans the deep six.</p><p>我们必须放弃所有计划。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f12a8d1265a3367103b7640612b9083c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"330\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f12a8d1265a3367103b7640612b9083c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;500&#39; height=&#39;330&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"330\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f12a8d1265a3367103b7640612b9083c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f12a8d1265a3367103b7640612b9083c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>3、In seventh heaven</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>它不是指“在第七天堂 ”而是说“十分高兴”</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>例句：</b></p><p>After I was given my first camera I was in seventh heaven.</p><p>我得到我的第一台照相机后开心极了。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>4、Have two left feet</b><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>它的意思不是“有两只左脚”而是“笨手笨脚，笨拙”谁会有两只左脚？歪果仁是不是数错啦？答案很简单：并没有。人家这是在形容“笨手笨脚”。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>例句：</b></p><p>My wife is a good dancer, but I&#39;ve got two left feet.</p><p>我太太舞跳得很好，可是我却笨手笨脚。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-c24979cd80dba87a3b6f27e0190ab99b_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1024\" data-rawheight=\"603\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1024\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-c24979cd80dba87a3b6f27e0190ab99b_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1024&#39; height=&#39;603&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1024\" data-rawheight=\"603\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1024\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-c24979cd80dba87a3b6f27e0190ab99b_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-c24979cd80dba87a3b6f27e0190ab99b_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>5、Ten to one</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>十对一，压倒性优势很明显。这个短语是“十之八九、非常有可能”的意思。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>例句：</b></p><p>Ten to one he&#39;ll be late.</p><p>他十有八九得迟到。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>Ten to one the teacher made a mistake.</p><p>很可能老师犯了一个错误。</p><p><b>----分割线------</b></p><p><b>切记：如果你想加入有外国人、大学生的英语社群，关注我的公众号“竖起耳朵听”英语角里</b>会伦敦腔、美音、印度腔的小伙伴都有！找到它就能一起交流。</p>",

            "content": "<p>翻译讲究音、形、义三方面完美神译原作，下面这篇《三字经》被网友称为史上最美汉英翻译，赶紧看看大神是如何用英语“传神达意”的吧！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ef669cc0ade5e630496cad06fbd33baf_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1024\" data-rawheight=\"768\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1024\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ef669cc0ade5e630496cad06fbd33baf_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1024&#39; height=&#39;768&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1024\" data-rawheight=\"768\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1024\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ef669cc0ade5e630496cad06fbd33baf_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ef669cc0ade5e630496cad06fbd33baf_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>1、人之初，性本善。性相近，习相远。</b></p><p>Man on earth,Good at birth.The same nature，Varies on nurture.</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>释义：</b></p><p>人出生之初，禀性本身都是善良的，只是后天环境不同和所受教育不同，彼此有了习性的差别。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>2、苟不教，性乃迁。教之道，贵以专。</b></p><p>With no education,There&#39;d be aberration.To teach well,You deeply dwell.<br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>释义：</p><p>如果从小不好好教育，善良的本性就会变坏。所以要专心一致地去教育孩子。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-dc9b90461fe84801671bc77ff5319a4f_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"8\" data-rawheight=\"5\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"8\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;8&#39; height=&#39;5&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"8\" data-rawheight=\"5\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"8\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-dc9b90461fe84801671bc77ff5319a4f_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>3、昔孟母，择邻处。子不学，断机杼。</b></p><p>Then Mencius&#39; mother，Chose her neighbor.At Mencius sloth,She cut the cloth.</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>释义：</p><p>孟子的母亲曾三次搬家，是为了使孟子有个好的学习环境。一次孟子逃学，孟母就折断了织布的机杼来教育孟子。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>4、子不教，父之过。教不严，师之惰。</b></p><p>What&#39;s a father?A good teacher.What&#39;s a teacher?A strict preacher.</p><p>释义：</p><p>仅仅是供养儿女吃穿，而不好好教育，是父母的过错。只是教育，但不严格要求就是做老师的懒惰了。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-0f165cc6171199f72a243276099b32e5_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"375\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-0f165cc6171199f72a243276099b32e5_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;500&#39; height=&#39;375&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"375\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-0f165cc6171199f72a243276099b32e5_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-0f165cc6171199f72a243276099b32e5_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>5、玉不琢，不成器。人不学，不知义。</b></p><p>No jade crude,Shows craft good.Unless you learn,Brute you&#39;ll turn.</p><p>释义：</p><p>玉不打磨雕刻，不会成为精美的器物；人若是不学习，就不懂得礼仪，不能成才。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>6、为人子，方少时。亲师友，习礼仪。</b></p><p>Son of man,Mature you can.Teacher or peer,Hold them dear.</p><p>释义：</p><p>做儿女的，从小时候就要亲近老师和朋友，以便从他们那里学习到许多为人处事的礼节和知识。</p><p><b>----分割线------</b></p><p><b>切记：如果你想加入有外国人、大学生的英语社群，关注我的公众号“竖起耳朵听”英语角里</b>会伦敦腔、美音、印度腔的小伙伴都有！找到它就能一起交流。</p>",
